External Report on Recent Diplomatic Trends

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Bao Jing'an of the Information Department to the Central Broadcasting Station this morning (the 18th) to report on the recent diplomatic situation as follows:

"In the past week, the diplomatic aspects had quite important content. There are roughly the following types of events: (1) Sino-Russian Negotiations: Currently, the Chinese representative in Moscow is still in contact with Karakhan and may make further negotiations. As for the current negotiations regarding the release of overseas Chinese detained in Russia, a brief report can also be made. Recently, the Foreign Affairs Department received a report from the Consul-General in Vladivostok, stating that it had received a letter from the Russian negotiator stationed in Vladivostok, saying that except for 23 overseas Chinese who were still in custody due to criminal sanctions, all other overseas Chinese had been released. However, after investigation, the families of the overseas Chinese who the Russian side claimed to have been released firmly stated that they had not been released. Therefore, it is quite difficult to investigate for a while. As for the reasons why the investigation is not easy, there are roughly the following types: (1) After the overseas Chinese are detained, when their families report to the German Consulate and the Chinese Consulate, the names and Russian transliterations are often inconsistent, or even the overseas Chinese fabricate false names to avoid certain suspicions after being detained, resulting in the Russian side not being able to find the person after several investigations based on the list sent by our consulate. (2) After the Russian side detains the overseas Chinese, it first asks for their names, ages, etc., compiles a list, and assigns code numbers. From then on, it refers to them by code number. When sending them to work elsewhere, it calls out their code numbers and sends them separately. Overseas Chinese who are unwilling to go to work elsewhere often secretly change code numbers, so that although their relatives know for sure that they are in a certain place, the Russian side's investigation according to code number often does not match the names. (3) When overseas Chinese who were originally detained in a certain place are sent to work elsewhere, some escape midway, and some return to the country privately after being released because they are closer to the border. The individuals themselves and their relatives often do not report to the consulate, so it is impossible to verify whether the overseas Chinese have regained their freedom for a while. (4) After the overseas Chinese are detained, their relatives and friends may have reported to the consulate, but when the consulate inquires at the address of the relatives and friends, they have either returned to the country or moved elsewhere, making it impossible to investigate. The above situations are the most difficult reasons for this negotiation. Currently, our consulates in Russia are re-investigating thoroughly in order to jointly negotiate and achieve the purpose of releasing the detained overseas Chinese. As for the negotiation to return the detained overseas Chinese's property, according to a letter from the Russian negotiator, it has been confiscated by the customs according to the example of attempted smuggling. After active negotiations by our Consul-General in Vladivostok, the Russian side finally agreed that except for the property carried by overseas Chinese who returned to the country through Vladivostok and deemed to be smuggled by the customs, which cannot be returned according to law, all other property seized during the road case should be returned together, except for contraband. Currently, our Consul-General in Vladivostok has opened a list and asked the Russian side to return the items that should be returned first, so that they can be transferred to the original owners, and the rest will be negotiated later. (2) League of Nations Issues: The 11th General Assembly of the League of Nations has been scheduled to be held in Geneva on September 11 this year. In order for our country to be elected as a member of the Council at this session, we have ordered Minister Wu in the United States and ministers in other countries to contact the governments of the countries where they are stationed. According to reports, more and more countries are sympathetic to our country's election this time, and there is a good chance of being elected this time. As for the candidates for representatives of our country to the General Assembly, the National Government specially appointed Ministers Wu Chaochu, Jiang Zuobin, and Gao Lu as members on the 11th. At last year's League of Nations General Assembly, China was also represented by the three ministers, who made great achievements. In particular, Minister Wu advocated the implementation of Article 19 of the League Covenant, which is closely related to our country's abolition of unequal treaties. Therefore, the three ministers will be sent to attend this session. As for the credentials, the National Government can issue them in a few days and send them separately by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The Foreign Affairs Department has already telegraphed the Chinese representative office of the League of Nations to inform the League of Nations Secretariat of the situation of the designated representatives. (3) Protection of Overseas Chinese and Party Affairs: (1) Japan: It is found that Japan has recently been declining in both industry and commerce, and factories and commercial institutions have been implementing layoffs and reducing government, resulting in an increasing number of unemployed workers in Japan. As a result, Chinese workers in Japan are also affected. In order to protect its own workers, the Japanese government has imposed extremely strict restrictions on the entry of Chinese workers, and has even deported Chinese workers. Therefore, in addition to ordering Minister Wang in Japan to raise serious negotiations with the Japanese government based on the principle of reciprocity in order to achieve the purpose of canceling restrictions, the Foreign Affairs Department also separately ordered the Minister in Japan and the Consuls-General in Yokohama, Kobe, and Korea to investigate unemployed Chinese workers in Japan, try to send them back to China in batches, and inform coastal provinces to investigate and prohibit traffickers from sending workers abroad, so as to avoid vagrancy and to prevent the establishment of facts. (2) British Malaya: Since Governor Kim Wen-tai of Singapore banned activities with high-pressure means, the Foreign Affairs Department telegraphed the Minister in England and the Consul-General in Singapore to conduct strict negotiations with the British government and the New Territories authorities, respectively. The British Colonial Office is still investigating. Recently, the local government of Muar in British Malaya has arrested party members. The Foreign Affairs Department has protested the case. (3) Dutch East Indies: The Dutch East Indies' oppression of party affairs is roughly the same as that of the British East Indies. The use of party doctrine textbooks in Chinese schools has always been prohibited. After repeated negotiations by the Foreign Affairs Department with the embassy in the Dutch East Indies and the Consul-General in Java, they have now allowed the free import of party doctrine books. As for the restriction that members of the Party Department cannot hold teaching positions, it also stems from the Dutch Governor's ban. The Consul-General in Java, Zhang, is actively negotiating with the Dutch Governor. (4) Establishment of Consulates in Nicaragua, Central America: There are many Chinese residents operating in Nicaragua. Because our country has not yet signed a treaty with Nicaragua and has not yet exchanged envoys, there is no establishment of a consulate, and the overseas Chinese also lack proper protection. The Foreign Affairs Department has now obtained the consent of the Nicaraguan government to establish a consulate, and has ordered Li Shizhong, the Acting Agent in Panama, to personally go to Nicaragua to investigate the situation. (5) Siam: Recently, the Foreign Affairs Department reported that 29 people were arrested at the May 1st Commemoration Day celebration held by the branch in Siam. After the branch tried to negotiate, all were released on bail pending trial. It is found that the Siamese government has repeatedly interfered in the affairs of overseas Chinese and has repeatedly requested improvements, but the other party has always replied with empty words without any results. The May 1st Labor Day is a world-wide holiday, and commemorative speeches are a matter of customary practice. Why should they be arrested at will? Although they have been released on bail, the original case has not been dismissed, which is very inappropriate. The Foreign Affairs Department has telegraphed Minister Wang in Japan to protest to the Siamese Ambassador in Japan."

Xu Zushan Talks about Receiving Weihai

Details of the Reception Have Been Negotiated and Compromised

It Will Be Managed According to the City System after Reception

Qingdao Communication - After the Sino-British signing of the Weihaiwei Return Agreement, the Central Commission appointed Xu Zushan as the Special Commissioner for the Reception of Weihai and set October 1 as the date for implementation of the reception. After receiving the order, Mr. Xu went to Weihai in person last month to investigate the local situation in Weihai and to negotiate the details of the reception with the British Minister in Weihai. Mr. Xu has been in Weihai for more than 20 days. The results of the contact were very satisfactory. Now that the matter is over, he took the Kyodo Maru No. 21 from Weihai and arrived in Qingdao today (14th) and stayed at the Naval Jianxing Society on Zhongshan Road. I especially went to visit him. Mr. Xu's conversation is as follows: "The most important purposes of my visit to Weihai this time are about two items. First, the return of Weihai. What is stipulated in the central treaty is all a general outline, and all paper items need to be specified in detail with the British Minister in Weihai. During my stay in Weihai for more than 20 days, I met with the British Minister in Weihai, Johnston, several times. Mr. Johnston was able to be open and honest about all the procedures, and the details of the reception were negotiated and compromised by both parties. There will be no difficulties when receiving in the future. Second, investigate the situation of the British administration of Weihai and the local conditions in preparation for the reception and to predetermine the policy after the reception. I found that the area is small and it is a free trade port. Commerce is not very developed. After the reception, attention must be paid to finance. Under the British administration of the area, the British government had a specific subsidy, so it was able to maintain the status quo. The area originally stationed a regiment of British troops, now only about 100 people left. After the reception, they can be withdrawn within one month as stipulated in the treaty. However, the security issue after the recovery must be properly handled to avoid giving people an excuse. As for municipal affairs, it is necessary to report to the central government for instructions before they can be stipulated. Roughly speaking, it should be handled in accordance with the city organization law promulgated by the central government." It is heard that Mr. Xu intends to stay in Qing for a short time and then take a wheel south to report everything to the central government (July 14).

Plans for Guangdong Province to Issue Post-War Recovery Bonds

Totaling 15 Million Yuan to be Sold in Four Tranches

Weekly Interest of 8 Percent, Secured by Provincial Revenue

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has suffered from years of war, with huge military expenses. The financial authorities often lament their empty coffers. The miscellaneous taxes borne by the people have not yet been lifted. After the resolution of the Guangxi war, it was thought that Guangdong Province could recuperate. Unexpectedly, soon after the Guangxi affair was settled, there was a major battle in southern Hunan. After the Hunan war came to an end, the remaining troops of the Guangxi army retreated back to Guangxi, and the Eighth Route Army returned west, and now Guangxi Province has once again become a place of continuous war. As a result, Guangdong Province's supplies are almost exhausted. The entire province's administrative expenses have been affected. Recently, the Finance Department has strictly limited the Chamber of Commerce to clear the military bonds sold by various shops within a week. However, the total amount of these military bonds is 4 million yuan, which has been sold by various parties, and it is said that they will soon be cleared. In order to cope with the current situation, the Finance Department recently plans to issue 15 million yuan of local post-war recovery bonds for the 19th year of the Republic of China, in the name of handling post-war affairs and maintaining the central banknotes. The Finance Department has drafted a statement of opinions, which will be submitted to the provincial affairs meeting for review and implementation tomorrow (the 15th). Judging from the current situation, this proposal should be passed and implemented, because the military situation is still pressing, and there is an urgent need for funds, and various 5-yuan and 10-yuan banknotes of the Central Bank also need to be restored to cash payment. Without specific funds, it is really difficult to cope with. The following is the statement of reasons for issuing the post-war recovery bonds drafted by the Finance Department: Since this province launched troops to suppress the rebellion in May of last year, it has been more than a year. Expenditures have increased sharply due to military affairs, and income has been shortened due to military affairs. All the assets of the national and provincial treasuries are still insufficient to supply military expenses. Therefore, advance collection of taxes, advance borrowing of various taxes, issuance of military bonds, additional collection of one-tenth of silver coins, and raising industrial rent have been used. Everything that can raise funds has been done. However, it is like a cup of water trying to put out a burning cart of wood, and it dries up before it is full. Although the military affairs in the two Guangs have come to an end, the amount of supplies and pay has not decreased. Bonds and borrowing are difficult to repay, and tax deductions are not enough. If no measures are taken as soon as possible, the provincial treasury will be exhausted, and the administration will be suspended. How can we take care of the aftermath? It is found that the payment orders issued by this department before the end of June this year, but not yet paid, amount to more than 1.1 million yuan. The expenses of various agencies in June that should be issued payment orders are no less than 1 million yuan. In addition, the necessary administrative expenses in July are more than 1 million yuan, and the funds for the principal and interest of military bonds paid on behalf of the national treasury for military expenses require about 1.7 million yuan. The total amount of funds to be paid by the provincial treasury is 5.34 million yuan. The total amount of funds that can be collected in July, such as fundraising and taxes, is about 1.1 million yuan, which is not enough to pay the various payment orders issued before the end of June. As for the administrative expenses for June and July, the military expenses for July, and the bond funds, etc., at least 4.23 million yuan are required, and it is not known where to get it from. This is only in terms of July. In the future, the implementation of the elimination of taxes will reduce more than 1 million yuan per month, and the difficulty is even more unknown. I believe that the way to manage finances is nothing more than increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. At this time, all industries are declining and the people are exhausted. It is not easy to implement new taxes. Even the sand fields being cleared and organized everywhere and the declaration of farmland may not increase income, but the effect is not visible, and it is too slow to solve the urgent need. Although there is room for savings in the administrative expenses of this province, the military expenses have not been reduced. Even if the administrative expenses can be reduced to the lowest limit, it is still not enough to help the matter, and because the value of the central currency is low, and the financial activities of the Central Bank have not yet started, there is no way to contribute. After repeated deliberations, the only feasible way is to continue to borrow from merchants and people. The only problem is that the old debts have not been cleared, and new debts have accumulated. The first, second, and third-phase public bonds and financial bonds borrowed from foreign banks and local banks amount to no less than 30 to 40 million yuan. If it is not cleared for a long time, the credibility of merchants and people to the government has long been weak, and there is no considerable collateral or definite guarantee. It is very difficult to get them to actively respond. However, if you want to give up this and make other plans, you really have no long-term strategy. The only way to deal with the current situation is to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance to find a way to clear the old debts to restore the previous credibility, and to raise funds from the Ministry to replenish the treasury and repay the new debts, and at the same time maintain the banknotes and consolidate the finance. It is planned to issue 15 million yuan of Guangdong post-war recovery bonds in the 19th year of the Republic of China. (The following is omitted) Attached: Regulations on post-war recovery bonds. Article 1: This bond is named Guangdong Post-War Recovery Bond, and the principal and interest are guaranteed by the revenue of the Guangdong Provincial Treasury. Article 2: The quota of this bond is 15 million yuan in Guangdong silver dollars. Article 3: The purpose of this bond is to clear the short-term military bonds issued in the 18th year of the Republic of China, replenish the treasury, and maintain the currency. Article 4: The interest rate of this bond is set at 8% per week, calculated every six months. Article 5: This bond will be issued in August of the 19th year of the Republic of China. Article 6: This bond will be issued at full face value, but in order to encourage those who pay early, if the payment is made before September 15th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, they will be allowed to pay 50% of the unredeemed banknotes of the Guangdong Central Bank. 30% before October 15th, 20% before November 15th, and full cash will be collected after this date. However, those who pay within the aforementioned time limit will be allowed to deduct handling fees as follows: (A) The first phase, before September 15th, deduct 5%; (B) The second phase, before October 15th, deduct 4%; (C) The third phase, before November 15th, deduct 3%; (D) The fourth phase, after November 16th, deduct 2%. However, the issuance of expenses and the overdue period shall not be deducted. Article 7: Six months after the issuance of this bond, the principal and interest will be repaid in equal installments over 15 months. The order will be determined by lottery. Article 8: The repayment of principal and interest of this bond will be managed by the Guangdong Central Bank. Article 9: The principal and interest fund to be paid for this bond shall be allocated by the Guangdong Finance Department from the provincial treasury revenue every month before the start of repayment of principal and interest, and shall be deposited by the Guangdong Central Bank for disbursement. Article 10: This bond is set as unregistered. Article 11: This bond is divided into four types: 100 yuan, 50 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan, but a part of the 5 yuan bond is made into five shares, each share is 1 yuan, so as to facilitate the distribution of odd numbers. Article 12: This bond may be freely mortgaged and traded, and may be used as a guarantee reserve for banks, and other public guarantees. Article 13: Those who forge this bond and damage its credibility shall be punished according to law. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Evening of July 14th)

Verdict in the Case of Postal Workers Transporting Opium in Liaoning Province

Shenyang Correspondence: Two cases of personnel from the Liaoning-Ningbo Postal Administration trafficking in opium have been tried by the court for many days, and the verdicts have now been announced. One case was the discovery of empty bags, and the other was the exposure of a contract. The first group of defendants, Shen Tianjue, Zhao Guofeng, and Han Shuren, were found guilty based on the empty opium bags, and the facts of the crime were obvious. Shen Tianjue was sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan. Zhao Guofeng and Han Shuren were each sentenced to two years of imprisonment and fined 400 yuan. The second group of defendants, Du Shichang, Zhang Fengchi, and Xu Jingyi, were found guilty based on the contract. Du Shichang has admitted that the contract was written by him, and Zhang and Xu also admitted that there was a contract. However, they argued that the contract was for transporting soil or selling green vegetables and fruits. The court judged the meaning of the contract and believed that it was definitely not for green vegetables and fruits, and there was no doubt that it was for transporting opium. Although it is not known how many times they continued to transport, according to Du Shichang's defense, the contract was not actually implemented. According to normal business, it is necessary to prepare everything before signing a contract, and there is a clause that it has already come into effect, so it should be considered completed, not attempted. Therefore, Du Shichang and Zhang Fengchi were each sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan, and Xu Jingyi was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 100 yuan. It is said that Shen, Du, and others are not satisfied and will appeal. (11th)

Xu Xiongzhang Talks About the Russian Confiscation of Overseas Chinese Property

Houses Allowed to be Claimed Within Six Months

More Than 20,000 Overseas Chinese Still Working in Russia

Harbin Correspondence: At 2:30 this afternoon, Xu Xiongzhang, the Consul General in Vladivostok, Russia, arrived in Harbin to pick up his family. Xu took office in early February of this year. After taking office, he was handling the matter of the confiscation of overseas Chinese property. He has already made some progress in the negotiations. He will stay in Harbin for about two or three days, and then return to his post. The reporter met him at his friend Lu Tai's place. Xu talked about the process of handling the return of overseas Chinese property as follows: First of all, there were about 200 houses in Vladivostok owned by overseas Chinese, with a total value of more than 3 million Russian rubles. After the Sino-Russian Incident on July 11th last year, Russia ordered the arrest of homeowners. Most of the overseas Chinese owners were arrested and imprisoned, and the rest fled back to their home countries. All 200 houses were managed by the Vladivostok Municipal Bureau, and it was announced that if no one claimed them within six months from the date of confiscation, they would be confiscated. In fact, this kind of officialdom was just a means to cover up their looting. The overseas Chinese who fled back to their home countries did not dare to claim them, and those who were imprisoned had no way to claim them. As a result, only a empty favor was given. Later, the Khabarovsk Agreement was signed, and the imprisoned overseas Chinese were released. Some of them went to the Municipal Bureau to claim their property. The Russian side did not want to go back on its word because the six-month deadline had not yet expired, so it returned the property. It is estimated that about 100 houses were claimed. The remaining 30 or so houses were still managed by the Municipal Bureau on behalf of the owners because the owners had returned to their home countries and no one came to claim them. Xu took office this spring. As the six-month deadline was approaching, he negotiated with the Russian side to extend the deadline for claiming. He obtained Russian permission to start counting six months from the date of the Khabarovsk Agreement. Xu took office about four or five months after the Khabarovsk Agreement was signed. If he followed the procedures to notify the owners to come and claim them, there would not be much time left. Therefore, he still contacted the Russian side and negotiated to check the number of unclaimed houses, conclude an agreement, and from the date of the agreement, recruit people to claim them, or allow them to entrust someone to claim them. If no one came to claim them after six months, Russia would be allowed to confiscate them. This method seems to be appropriate. Xu will handle it when he returns to his post from Harbin. As for the overseas Chinese in Russia, there are still more than 20,000 people, all of whom maintain their livelihoods by working. The Russian side benefits from their diligence and cheap wages, and is more willing to hire them, so the Chinese workers can still support their lives. The abuse is not as serious as rumored outside. As for the exit passport, the procedures are troublesome. This is not only the case for overseas Chinese, but also for overseas citizens of other countries. (11th)

Hangzhou Waterworks Signs Contract for Water Supply Network

Siemens Company Wins Bid

The Hangzhou Waterworks Preparatory Committee officially opened the bidding for the thirteenth section of the water supply network on May 1st. All the bids were handed over to the engineering department of the committee for sorting and signing. For the sake of prudence, engineering experts from various agencies were specially invited to form a bid review committee. After several reviews, the price of Siemens Company was the lowest. The fifteenth temporary meeting of the committee decided that Siemens Company would win the bid and recommended committee members Wang Zuyao, Wang Xirong, Jin Runquan, and Zhang Facheng to contact Xu Lan, the representative of Siemens Company, to discuss payment methods and negotiate the contract. The contract was officially signed on the 16th of this month by Zhu Jiahua, the chairman of the committee, members Wang Xile, Wang Zuyao, Jin Runquan, Zhang Facheng, and Xu Lan, the representative of Siemens Company. The total price of the contract is US$137,195.20. The first phase of material costs and insurance costs from Shanghai to Hangzhou have also been paid on the same day in accordance with the contract, totaling US$14,491.24. In addition, the engineering experts from various agencies have reviewed and decided that the pumping station for the twelfth section will be awarded to Jebsen & Co. The total price of the contract is £1,784. The formal contract will be officially signed after the committee meeting. As for the construction of the general plant of Sanhe, since the advertisement for bidding was published on the 10th of this month, contractors from all over the country have come to inquire or collect bids. The committee decided to officially open the bidding at 10:00 am on the 31st of this month. (Daily News)

Local Correspondence

Jiading

Liquor Case Appealed: Zhou Weixin's liquor shop outside Ximen was previously reported to the Public Security Bureau by Jin and others for selling liquor. The case of searching and suing each other has been heard by the county government. The seized liquor has been sent to the Shanghai Central Health Experiment Institute for testing, and it has been found to be non-toxic. Now, Zhou has filed an appeal with the High Court due to heavy losses. The High Court has accepted the case and will extract the entire case file from the county for review and handling soon.

Change of Autonomous Region: The autonomous region of this county was originally divided into eight districts. Now, due to the disparity in the size of the regions, there are many obstacles. (That is, in terms of funding, the smaller ones only have more than 40 yuan per month, and the income is insufficient. It has been in arrears for several months.) The county administrative meeting has previously decided to submit a request to the Civil Affairs Department for approval to change the case and re-divide it. The Department has approved it, but it should be implemented after the citizens of each district swear in and register, and the election of township heads is completed to avoid disputes. The plan to divide the six districts proposed by the former District Committee has been sent to the Department for record.

Chuansha

Director of Construction Bureau Abandons Post and Flees: Li Jingzhao (Guangdong native), the Director of the Construction Bureau of Chuansha County, has been commissioned to Chuansha for a year and a half since last spring. He has been working diligently, but he is addicted to opium, and it is inconvenient to smoke, so he often stays in Shanghai. In May of this year, the county party department sent a letter to the county government requesting that Li be transferred for inspection. Li went to the county to request a postponement of the date, so that he could go to Shanghai for medical treatment. Later, County Magistrate Ruan approved the postponement until the 15th of this month to come to the county for inspection. After receiving the order, Li continued to work as usual. Unexpectedly, he went to Shanghai at the end of last month and never returned. The heads of the technical section, Sun Songxian, and the general affairs section, Zhang Luo, went to Shanghai one after another to investigate at Li's relatives and friends, but found nothing. After returning without results, the staff of the bureau consulted and decided that the matter was too important to be covered up, so they went to the county to report at about 7 pm on the 17th and requested instructions on how to deal with it. County Magistrate Ruan ordered the important staff in the bureau to provide guarantees and wait outside for instructions. Only Wu Weiyuan, a native of Guangdong, who was in charge of general affairs in the bureau, was not guaranteed and was ordered to be sent to the Public Security Bureau for temporary custody. Early in the morning of the 18th, Zhong Menglin, a member of the second section and concurrently an accountant, was sent to the Construction Bureau to check the files, accounts, and equipment. At the same time, the Public Security Bureau was ordered to send two policemen to guard the bureau. Also, the construction funds stored in the Shanghai Bank of Communications were very large, about 18,000 yuan. Fearing that there would be a case of forging seals and stealing, he took a car to Shanghai on the morning of the same day (18th) to inquire about everything.

Taizhou

Establishment of Rice Export Inspection Office: The preparation for the Rice Export Inspection Office in Haimen, Linhai has been long. The county government and the French election Xie Xinhai as the director of the office. It was officially established today (16th).

Great Flood: The weather in Linhai has been unusually hot recently. On the 13th of this month, there was a sudden hurricane and rain. The next day, the water in the four countryside was several feet full. It did not recede until the 15th. The loss of crops and grains and ships was very large. After years of floods, this catastrophe has been encountered again, and the poor people are crying bitterly.

Songjiang

Confessions of Robbers in Sijing: Yesterday, the county government sent political police chief Dong Dingtang to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to bring back thirteen male and female bandits, including Lin Zicheng, who looted the town of Sijing. The case was heard by the judge Du Chengshen that evening. It is learned that the names of the bandits are Lin Zicheng, Zuo Shiqing, Zuo Shenggen, Liu Zhizhong, Wang Dequan, Gan Degui, Mao Ziqing, Wang Cangyou, Xu Yupu, Wang Tongyou, Hong Zuojiang, and female bandits Shen Lu's and Zhang Wang's. First, Lin Zicheng confessed that after the robbery, he divided the spoils and got half a piece of foreign money, totaling 50 yuan. He admitted it without hesitation. Mao Ziqing did not admit to being the bandit leader. When asked who was holding the Mao character banner at the time of the robbery, he claimed that he did not know. The confessions of the other bandits were mostly denials. Shen Lu's, the wife of the deceased Ding Lao, who was hiding firearms, had 40 guns and two boxes of bullets seized, and admitted that the bandit Ding had kidnapped Zhu in Chonggu and hid him in her house. After the interrogation, each of them drew their confessions and were taken into custody.

Captain Pan Seized Gangster: Pan Baozhong, the captain of the Fourth Smuggling Suppression Brigade, who is stationed in the Punan coastal area, is very good at suppressing bandits. He seized bandits in Wanxunqiao South the other day. At 1 pm on the 17th, he happened to encounter a large group of bandits who resisted arrest, relying on their numbers. Captain Pan shot and killed one person on the spot and detained four people, seizing one Mauser pistol and one pistol each. More than 100 remaining bandits scattered to the south. Mr. Pan personally led Captain Tan and Deputy Captain Tao to pursue and suppress them. It is learned that the four captured bandits, Zhang Heshang, a native of Qianwei, Yao Yinhe, a native of Pinghu, Chen Azhao, a native of Pinghu Xinmiao, and Tang Arong, a native of Jinshan Tagang, were taken back to the brigade headquarters. After a preliminary interrogation, it is heard that they will be sent back to Jinshan for investigation. The bandit who was killed was Yu Arong, a native of Liu Jiawei Bridge, Jinshan, and it is heard that he was a notorious bandit under TaiBao Ashu.

Four Bandits Arrested in Xiaoliangting: The County Public Security Bureau reported that four bandits were escorted from the First Branch of Tinglin to Songjiang and transferred to the County Government for handling. According to reports from informants in the Tinglin Branch, the bandits Hua Baogen, Hua Caisheng, Xu Axiang, etc., have now sneaked back to Xiaoliangting and are active in the Dian Shan Mapeng area. Hua Baogen has been involved in many robbery cases in the southern countryside. Branch Chief Pan led the police to Hua Baogen's house in Xiaoliangting and searched but found nothing. Later, Hua Baogen and Hua Caisheng were seized in the pig shed behind the house. Two people carrying chisels and hemp ropes were encountered on the way. After being arrested, they confessed that they were Zhang Asi and Zhang Asheng. After returning to the bureau, Hua Baogen and Hua Caisheng confessed that they had robbed with Xu Axiang, etc. Zhang Asi confessed to stealing dew objects. Zhang Asheng also admitted to stealing, and also admitted to robbing Xu Hongsheng's house in Caojing with Chen Asi in November last year, etc.

Suzhou

Problem of the Chamber of Commerce Stopping Activities: The Suzhou General Chamber of Commerce is reorganizing according to the Chamber of Commerce Law and the Industrial and Commercial Guild Law, and has submitted a request to the county party department for registration. The party department ordered the General Chamber of Commerce to maintain the status quo for the time being because the guilds of various industries are currently undergoing reorganization. Recently, the provincial party department decided that all old chambers of commerce should stop activities and be received or managed by the local party departments. As a result, fundamental problems have arisen in the Chamber of Commerce. It is heard that the local Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce yesterday, and has submitted a request to the provincial department for explanation on the remaining matters. However, the local Chamber of Commerce has not yet made a statement.

Negligence of Steamboat Sailor Caused Disaster: The Laogongmao steamboat traveling to and from Suzhou Mudong has wharfs to rely on in Hengtang, Xikuatang, etc. On the 17th, Zhao Yuan, the wife of Ma Sanbao, who lived in Xitang, took the steamboat from the city to return home. When the steamboat reached Xikuatang, the sailor saw that only Zhao Yuan was getting off the boat, so he was lazy and did not bring the boat close to the wharf, and only drove slowly without stopping. At that time, Zhao Yuan was carrying a heavy burden and could not jump far, so she lost her footing and fell on the wharf board, and both feet fell into the water. Seeing this, the steamboat started to dock. Unexpectedly, one of Zhao Yuan's feet was crushed by the boat, and she fainted from the pain. After being helped back home, she soon died of her injuries. After her death, blue marks were also found on her abdomen and chest, and the situation was terrible.

Suzhou Continues to Search and Arrest Reactionaries: In addition to Wei Junhong (also known as Wei Junhong) and Jiang Weixi of Yueyi Girls' School, Zhang Yimin, a teacher at Chunshen Primary School, Ge Naibin and Wang Menglv, teachers in the city, Yang Zhongxian, a girl scout in Zhongshan, and Cai Zhihua in Chuanfang Lane, etc., who were arrested, the Public Security Bureau was ordered by the county government to search for firearms in a certain tea shop outside Changmen, Suzhou Central Primary School, and Nanchansi, etc. As a result, 70 to 80 reactionary books were found in the home of Gu Linfan (a teacher at Xiangcheng Primary School) at No. 35 Liuxiang, and 50 to 60 printed materials such as introduction letters and organizations of the "Joining the Tongmenghui" were found in the dormitory of a school in the city.

Robbery and Injury Case in Xihua Township: At 1 am yesterday (18th), more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to the house of Hua Shijin, a resident of Danjiazuiz, Xihua, and broke into the house, robbing 350 foreign dollars and clothes, etc., and injuring Hua's wife Zhou. Zhou has come to Suzhou City Hospital for treatment.

Wuxi

The Silk Factory Disturbance of Unclear Truth There are a total of forty-nine silk factories in the city. In Lihua Village outside the North Gate, there are Yuanfeng, Wanyi, and Yiyi factories. In Zhou Shanbang, there are Wufeng, Deda, Yuchang, and Ruichang factories. Yesterday morning (the 18th), after factories such as Yuanfeng and Wanyi called for a strike, only a small number of workers went to work. The rest gathered around the North New Bridge area, firmly refusing to work. The truth is unclear. The Yiyi factory, which originally made one-corner [yarn], continued to work as usual, but dismissed its workers after 9 a.m. When the female workers gathered at the North New Bridge, a rumor spread, and a group of female workers went to the Ruichang Silk Factory in Zhou Shanbang, persuading them to stop working. That factory stopped working immediately. It is unknown how, but a window was slightly damaged. The other Wufeng factory also stopped working, while Deda and Yu continued to work as usual. A group of female workers then entered that factory. With so many people and hands, it is unknown how, but the accounting room was destroyed. That factory also had to stop working. The situation was about to spread to the Qian Sheng Silk Factory under Gongyun Bridge, but fortunately, the police force was already on the scene, preventing it from spreading. Later, the female workers from each factory sent representatives to report to the Silk Factory Workers' Union, saying that when the management paid wages the day before yesterday (the 17th), they did not deduct union dues on their behalf, claiming that the union had been cancelled, and that they had increased the rent, which was contrary to the old agreement. This morning, a group of female workers misunderstood their words, leading to this misunderstanding. They requested a solution, etc. After receiving the report, the standing committee members of the union, Tao Shensheng, Hua Nianzu, and Ye Qiaoyun, immediately sent the investigation section to investigate, and also went to the county to meet with County Magistrate Sun, reporting everything, and instructing the sub-unions to resume work immediately. However, the female workers had already dispersed, and it was feared that they would not be able to resume work that day. The silk factories such as Deda and Yu also sent a letter to the Silk Factory Guild, requesting a solution. According to the factory side, this disturbance was actually caused by the spread of rumors. There was no ill will between labor and management. As for the destruction of Deda and Yu, it was because there was anger from the labor unrest last month, so resentment was unavoidable, leading to the repercussions. Whether it can be resolved depends on what happens today.

Detailed Record of the Dismissal of Patrol Chiefs Incident The third branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the South Gate of this city was stirred by a disturbance yesterday due to the dismissal of two patrol chiefs. It is learned that Wang Tingshu, the director of the branch bureau, had just taken office the day before yesterday and was handling matters with unusual haste. In the afternoon of that day at 4:00 p.m., after gathering all the chiefs and police for a roll call and speech, he dismissed patrol chief Zhang Shaofu and Chen Junhua, the patrol chief of the Second Police Station of Xiatang, in the evening, and wanted to dismiss six to nine patrol officers. Zhang and Chen, feeling they had been unfairly dismissed, immediately went to the Public Security Bureau to petition. Director Xu instructed them to be sent to the bureau and reassured to continue their duties. Unexpectedly, at 6:00 a.m. yesterday morning, Zhang and Chen suddenly led a small number of police officers to the bureau, forcibly taking Director Wang out, claiming that everyone would go to the Public Security Bureau to speak. They were then escorted to the Public Security Bureau, shouting slogans such as "Down with Director Wang who uses private connections" along the way. Director Wang was injured in the chaos. Patrol chiefs Zhang Shaofu and Chen Junhua also suffered minor injuries. After both sides arrived at the Public Security Bureau, Director Xu ordered Director Wang to go to the Brothers Hospital for medical treatment first, and had Zhang and Chen watched. Unexpectedly, the patrol police outside the South Gate suddenly went on strike. Subsequently, Li Linshi, the director of the branch bureau, earnestly persuaded all the police officers, and they all returned to their posts. After the incident, Public Security Bureau Director Xu, in addition to sending Inspector Qian Tianxiong to the South Gate to conduct an on-site investigation, also ordered Li Linshi, a member of the bureau, to temporarily act as the director, and ordered Wu Quan and Liu Desheng, the patrol chiefs of the first and second branch bureaus, to be transferred to the South District to temporarily serve as patrol chiefs of the third branch bureau. At about 4:00 p.m., Director Wang and the two patrol chiefs, Zhang and Chen, all went to the county government to request an injury examination. Presiding Judge Yu opened a court for trial and ordered them all to return for medical treatment and await further handling after their injuries healed. Meanwhile, personnel were dispatched to investigate the truth of the incident.

Two Robberies Result in Seven Casualties Wang A'de, a farmer in Da'an Village near Wan'an Market, Sixteenth District, Xiyi, earned his living by farming and was poor. He had three sons and one daughter. Unexpectedly, around 11:00 p.m. the night before last, two robbers holding pistols and speaking with a northern accent suddenly broke into his house, forbidding any outcry, and demanding to know where the silver was hidden. They then ransacked the chests and cabinets, but found nothing. They fired a warning shot and left to the north. Wang A'de bravely chased after them and was shot three times by the robbers, falling to the side of a mound, barely alive. He was spotted by neighbors, who carried Wang back. His family hired a boat to send him to the city, but he died of his injuries yesterday morning. Also, at the home of Wu Kunshou, a farmer in Wuxiang, Bashi Bridge, Tianxia Market, Sixteenth District, more than ten robbers suddenly came the night before last, holding knives, sticks, and other weapons, breaking into the house and looting wildly. They stole 55 yuan in silver, 11 banknotes, one gold ring, clothing, etc. When the villagers heard the alarm, they immediately gathered and bravely pursued. The villagers were no match and six people, Wu Sanbao, Xinggen, Shoupeng, A'quan, Jinchang, and Hesheng, were injured by knives and sticks. After the police from the Twelfth Branch of the Public Security Bureau arrived, the robbers fled. One robber, Wang Fusheng, was captured by the police and sent to the General Bureau for interrogation. Wu Kunshou and the six injured villagers came to the city yesterday afternoon to report their injuries to the county. They were ordered to return for treatment and await the arrest of the fleeing robbers.

Jiangyin

Rice Shops Robbed in Xiqiao Xiqiao, located outside the East Gate, is only a short distance from the Public Security Bureau of the county government. At around 1:00 a.m. on the 16th, seven or eight robbers suddenly came from the back door of the Xu Wansheng Rice Shop, grabbing the mother of Xu Rongchen, the owner of the rice shop, and forcing her to hand over silver dollars. They robbed a total of 30 silver dollars, 400 small silver coins, 100,000 copper coins, one gold needle, and six pieces of clothing. After the robbery, they went to the Wu Yitai Rice Shop next door, robbing 5 silver dollars, 50 small silver coins, 3,000 copper coins, and one gold ring. After the robbery, they went east. Yesterday, after learning about it, Xing Songwen, the district head of the First District, reported to the county government that the robbers dared to loot so close to the city, causing extreme panic among the people, requesting the dispatch of police to garrison.

Provincial Order to Recover Tuition Fees from Student Police Who Caused Trouble The Civil Affairs Department received a report from Wang Dasui, the principal of the Police Academy, stating that on the 10th of this month, student police in the police training class were incited by a small number of people and suddenly went on strike, making demands. Now that the disturbance has subsided, it has been found that the student police led by Lu Wenyu and 16 others, except for Chen Sihai and Zhang Yunzhen who were leniently released, Bai Yushan, Zhou Guirong, and Li Cui, are on the run, and Chen Wenyu and 16 others have been handed over to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for investigation. Meanwhile, orders have been sent to various counties to recover clothing and tuition fees, and Lu Wenyu, the leader, is from Jiangyin, with the owner of Maofeng Store on Dongda Street, Lu Weiqing, as his guarantor. The Civil Affairs Department ordered County Magistrate Li to follow the instructions and recover the fees.

Striving to Abolish the Provincial Tax on Factory Cloth The factory cloth industry in Jiangyin has been developing for decades and is the best in Jiangsu Province. In recent years, the production capacity has weakened, and instead of seeking industrial development, the consumption capacity is strong, and foreign goods are purchased exclusively. In addition, there are many toll stations and heavy taxes. Jiangsu and Zhejiang are adjacent provinces, and transportation is convenient. A considerable amount of Jiangyin factory cloth is sold to Zhejiang. However, on May 1st of this year, Zhejiang Province specially set up a provincial tax bureau, and the import tax on factory cloth has increased from one to ten times. Qian Daren, the executive committee member of the Jiangyin Tonghui Factory Cloth Association, specially sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce through the County Chamber of Commerce, urging the Zhejiang provincial authorities to strive to abolish the provincial tax on factory cloth in order to maintain business and promote domestic goods.

Militiamen Misunderstand and Injure Police Officer County Magistrate Li received a secret report from Qiu Wubao, Zhang A'yu, Zhang Zitian, and 50 other people from Qiugangpai Village, Qiaoqi Township, stating that Zhu Linrui, the eldest son of Zhu Shaohong, a famous doctor in Fenggezhuang, who is serving as a tax collector, has embezzled public funds, additionally charged eight points, harbored gambling dens, colluded with the Baowei Tuan (Local Militia) Da Li and Xiao Li, and sold opium, etc. County Magistrate Li then issued a hand order to the Public Security Bureau, ordering Fan Yu, a patrol officer from the Sanguan Public Security Second Police Station, to go to Qiaoqi with four plainclothes police officers on the morning of the 16th to investigate whether Qiu Wubao was there. Two opium smokers, Xu Minggui and Zhao Xiaogen, were caught on the street. Zhao Xiaogen escaped after reaching the Tenth District Office. After contacting District Chief Xu Lianqu, they went to the Baowei Tuan. It was already 1:00 a.m. Li Liangbi, the outer guard, asked for the password because Fan and others were wearing plain clothes. Later, Lu Guanhao, the new coach, explained the reason. Patrol Officer Fan entered and searched the positions of the militiamen, but found no opium. Then they went to the district office. The Baowei Tuan searched in plain clothes and did not see any official documents. When they asked for the documents, Fan hid the documents in his bag and they were snatched away by Lai Mingchu, a member of the militia. In the chaos, Fan was beaten, suffering minor injuries to his right rib and left neck. District Chief Xu stopped them and sent Fan to the home of Zhen Chief Xu Weizu. Fan also lost his pistol and other items. Yesterday morning (the 17th), after District Chief Xu reported to County Magistrate Li, he sent the police team Ma Huaizhong to the countryside to investigate. Patrol Officer Fan was sent to the Gospel Hospital for treatment. In the afternoon, Ma's team returned to the city and brought militiamen Li Liangbi and Lai Mingchu to the city to be interrogated by the county.

The Issue of Opening Human-Powered Rickshaws Zhenjiang has an quota of 1,000 human-powered rickshaws, with a current balance of 325. Yangzhou

The Provincial Government Orders the Establishment of the Baowei Tuan (Local Militia) The Jiangdu County Government, in response to the provincial government's order to establish the Baowei Tuan, has been instructed to handle it automatically in each locality. According to the report, the county only has more than 200 members in the four rural areas, and the firearms are not fully equipped. Moreover, the rural farmers in the four rural areas have not yet opened their minds, and it is also the busy farming season, and the district offices are implementing citizen oath registration, making it difficult to handle. A special request was made to the provincial government to postpone it. It is heard that an instruction has been received, which states, "It is true that during the busy farming season, it is difficult to force the Tuan Ding who should be trained in each household to serve. However, the district's screening procedures can be carried out in accordance with the regulations. The district chiefs should still be strictly supervised to complete the reporting within the time limit."

The Fuyunfengshun Steamer Conflicts with the People The Jiangdu County Government previously reported to the Second District Office that the inland river water was vast, and the dikes on both sides of the area from Guazhou to Yangzi Bridge were severely damaged. Small steamers traveling back and forth would cause further damage, so it was requested that the county government follow the precedent of previous floods and inform the Zhenjiang Customs to strictly order each small steamer to stop and tow the ropes when passing through that area. Unexpectedly, the Fuyun Steamer Bureau's Fengshun small steamer passed through Yangzi Bridge at 2:00 p.m. yesterday (the 16th) and did not comply. Therefore, many people gathered there and forced it to stop, resulting in a conflict and mutual violence. A man named Ma Shidong was injured on the side of the people. The police team stationed there arrested Zhu Yintang, Ge Defa, Xu Xinmo, Hu Zhengtiao, and four other executives from the steamer, and sent them and the injured person to the court for legal resolution.

Another Batch of Wounded Soldiers Arrives The Twenty-Seventh Rear Hospital stationed in Yangzhou has transported wounded soldiers from the front line, totaling 833 people. Yesterday (the 15th), another batch of more than 500 people was transported from the front. The hospital here did not make prior arrangements for the treatment location for these wounded soldiers, so it was extremely busy temporarily. Subsequently, the county government temporarily designated the Yaoyang Match Factory in the South Gate as a temporary treatment location. This morning, County Magistrate Chen convened all the doctors of the Doctors' Association to find a way to send people to change dressings first.

Gaoyou

Impersonating Military Officer The son of Wu Chengyi in this county, Wu Yushan, previously impersonated Wu Ji, the deputy director of the logistics management office of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Headquarters, and spread rumors everywhere. He was arrested by the 266th Regiment in Huaiyin. The telegraph ordered the First Company of the First Battalion stationed in You to search Wu's residence. The company immediately went to Wu's residence with the Public Security Bureau and found several military supplies. Wu Yushan's father was then released on bail. It is now heard that the headquarters is concerned that Wu Zhan dared to impersonate a senior military officer and may have other intentions. The telegraph ordered the regiment to escort Wu to Beijing for interrogation. After receiving the telegraph, Commander Huang ordered a military officer to lead a platoon of soldiers to escort Wu to You and temporarily imprison him in the county prison, awaiting orders to be escorted to Beijing.

Qingjiang

The Panic of Villagers in Three Markets On the evening of the 13th, more than 100 people resembling new soldiers suddenly appeared in Xiaoying and other places on the north bank of the Yanhe River in the third district of Huaiyin. They had mismatched uniforms and various firearms. They came from Jiangjia Xiaowei in Siyang. For a time, the villagers were greatly alarmed and fled everywhere. The local village corps and the LianShui civil militia immediately joined forces and strengthened their defenses. The County Government Police Brigade and the Public Security Bureau repeatedly sent scouts to investigate and report that the group of bandits had come to negotiate surrender. Their leaders were said to be surnamed Lin or Dai. After inquiring from all sides, nothing was known beforehand, and the villagers were even more uneasy. Therefore, from Zhujiaji on the border of Huai and Lian in the east, to both sides of Dahong in the west, to Wangying Xiba in the south, and to Dingji in the north, within a radius of more than ten li, all the strong men and militia, numbering about a thousand or more, were armed and gathered to monitor them closely. Fortunately, there were no unexpected actions. It was not until the night of the 14th that the bandits left the north bank of the Yanhe River in the rain and fled to the fifth district. That night, the county police brigade also sent a cavalry patrol to assist the militia, and did not return until noon on the 15th. However, according to a report to the police brigade commander Zhu Lianfang, the group of bandits was still stationed in Caowei, north of Wulizhuang.

Military Police Conduct a Major Search Commander Huang of the 266th Regiment stationed in the area, because communist leaflets have been found in and out of Huaiyin County recently, and according to reports, there are many undesirable elements hiding, hoping to obstruct local security, sent a team to join the police brigade, public security bureau, and chamber of commerce at 3:00 a.m. on the 14th, dividing the city inside and outside into seven districts, to carry out a major search. They first gathered at the regiment headquarters and then searched separately. They also notified the wooden fences at the entrances of the streets and alleys inside and outside the city to open slowly. The search ended at dawn, and except for the discovery of a large number of opium cases, nothing else was found. It is heard that the officials are still not discouraged and may conduct a second or third search soon.

Zhongxing Town is Frightened Siyang County Zhongxing Town was originally a larger commercial port in Jiangbei, but after the Liu Weizhu Village, four miles west of the town, was broken by bandits, merchants and residents in the town have been unable to live in peace. Because the county seat is prosperous and has more thorough anti-bandit equipment, most of the middle-class families in Zhongzhen have moved to Siyang County to avoid bandits, except for the wealthiest who have moved to other counties.

Nantong

The First Batch of Wounded Soldiers Arrives in Tong The Nantong Thirty-First Rear Hospital was established on the 16th, with Cao You as the director, Yu Housheng as the director of medical affairs, Lang Kezhong as the director of pharmacy, and Gao Liang, Liu Dazhong, etc. as military doctors. The first batch of more than 700 wounded soldiers arrived at Tianshenggang on the Daji Steamer on the 17th. The second batch of 800 soldiers is scheduled to arrive on the 19th.

Two Torpedo Boats Run Aground at Tianshenggang The Hupeng and Husun torpedo boats were pushed by strong winds and rapid tides onto the shoals of Tianshenggang on the morning of the 15th, making it difficult to move. Workers are currently being hired to use barges to try to transport them.

The County's Financial Difficulties The local finances of Nantong are not enough to cover expenses, reaching more than 70,000 yuan. The current temporary short-term loan of 50,000 yuan has not yet been borrowed. The previous loans have now expired. Because there is no money to repay, an agreement has been reached with the creditors to extend the term for six months. Construction funds must be diverted and repaid in installments after the next busy season begins.

Rugao

Rugao City Declares Special Martial Law The county government, due to the serious situation of rampant bandits and communists in this county, announced special martial law on the 15th. The four city gates are closed every night at 8:00 p.m., and no one is allowed to pass through after 9:00 p.m. without a password. Traffic is cut off at 10:00 p.m., and visits to prisoners in the prison are restricted to prevent trouble.

The County-Run Farm is Attacked by Bandits At 10:00 p.m. on the 11th, the county-run farm in Zhongyi District, Rugao Jugang, was suddenly attacked by thirty to forty bandits, holding more than thirty rifles, to attack the garrison troops stationed at the farm. The Baowei Tuan (Local Militia) stationed there had been ordered to be transferred elsewhere the day before, and the staff of the farm had moved to Jugang due to the banditry. Therefore, the bandits did not commit any violence and fled to the southeast.

Jiaxing

Order to Investigate False Accusations The names Zhao Wenzhao, Wu Gaowei, Shen Qiming, Lu Feicheng, Yang Sizhai, Gao Zhen, and Shen Zhenxin in Jiaxing accused County Magistrate Jiang Zhicheng of colluding with local bullies and engaging in embezzlement, and filed a complaint with the Civil Affairs Department, which sent personnel to thoroughly investigate. It was found that the allegations were mostly exaggerated and not true. The accusers were also not using their real names. The Civil Affairs Department believed that the false accusations should be thoroughly investigated and sent the original complaint and investigation report to the county, ordering County Magistrate Jiang to investigate the real names of the false accusers and send them to the County Local Court for investigation in accordance with the law, to warn against troublemakers. Mo Runxun, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, was also accused by Chen Wanzhong of this county in a letter to the Civil Affairs Department. He was ordered to accurately investigate the matter and report back before being stripped of his post. County Magistrate Jiang, because the accuser did not indicate his address and contact information, could not inquire, so he posted a notice yesterday, ordering the accuser Chen Wanzhong to report to the government in person within seven days to be questioned, so that the matter could be verified. If he fails to arrive after the deadline, he will be treated as a false accuser.

Scheduled Meeting to Merge School Districts Jiaxing School District originally had 25 districts, with one school affairs committee member in each district to manage education in the entire district. Later, it was merged into nine districts, and school affairs in each district were managed by the autonomous committee members of that district. After the autonomy was suspended, the 25-district system was restored. Former Education Bureau Director Shen planned to divide it into eight school districts and appoint eight educators to preside over school affairs in the eight districts. Now, because the autonomous region has been determined to be seven districts, the current Director of Education, Jiang Jing, believes that the education district and the autonomous region must be consistent.

For the sake of less difficulty in handling affairs, he has already presented it to the provincial government, and a county education committee meeting will be convened to discuss the merger method, so that it can be implemented from the eighteenth year and benefit school affairs.

Hangzhou

Execution of Kidnapper The kidnapper Ma Haitang, a native of Sheng County, had previously colluded with others to kidnap Qiu Shousong's ten-year-old younger brother, Qiu Shoubao, in the Zhangjia Temple area of that county, demanding 600 yuan for his release. He again gathered bandits on the evening of November 18th of the same year in Hengzha An Village, Lin'an County, and kidnapped Zhou Quanfa's six-year-old son, Zhou Bingsheng, demanding ransom in a letter to be negotiated near Shiheli, Yuhang County. They were intercepted by soldiers ambushing there, and a pistol and bullets were found. Zhou Bingsheng was then beaten to death with stones by the remaining bandits. The Second Company of the Special Affairs Battalion of the Security Team sent Ma Haitang to the Security Office, which transferred him to the court. He was sentenced to death. At 8:00 a.m. yesterday, the 18th, the prosecutor was sent to sign for the prisoner, verify his identity, and escort him to the execution ground outside Qingbo Gate for execution by firing squad.

The Anti-Smuggling Bureau Reorganizes Camps into Teams Since Zhen Shaojie took over the Two Zhejiang Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Bureau, he has planned to reorganize the various camps into brigades, squadrons, and platoons in accordance with the anti-smuggling team organizational outline previously issued by the Ministry of Finance. A few days ago, Director Zhen went to Shanghai and asked Director Wen of the Anti-Smuggling Department of the Ministry of Finance about this matter, and it has been approved. Therefore, all camps are now ordered to follow the instructions, and the brigade commanders are appointed as follows: First Brigade Commander Shu Yan, Second Brigade Commander Ling Xichao, Third Brigade Commander Li Guogan, Fourth Brigade Commander Luo Qin, Fifth Brigade Commander Chen Shaohan, Sixth Brigade Commander Zhen Xiqiu, Seventh Brigade Commander Luo Zhuohan, Eighth Brigade Commander Zhu Xuchu, Ninth Brigade Commander Cai Qingjing, Tenth Brigade Commander Guo Yi.

Continued Allocation of Highway Public Bonds The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance previously used highway public bonds to borrow 300,000 yuan from various silver and money industries for construction needs, receiving 282,500 yuan in actual cash. It was to be repaid monthly from the construction funds that should be issued each month, with a term of ten months. Now, the term has not yet expired, but it is not far off. In addition to the 180,000 yuan that has been repaid, another 30,000 yuan was repaid yesterday, and a letter was sent to the silver and money industries to share the amount.

Ningbo

The 200,000 Municipal Loan Will Sign a Contract The Ningbo Municipal Government will continue to borrow a short-term construction public bond of 200,000 yuan, still using the wharf donation as collateral, with a monthly interest rate of 1.1%, and a term of seven years. It was later learned that the money industry agreed to lend 100,000 yuan, and the banking industry agreed to lend 75,000 yuan, leaving a shortfall of 25,000 yuan, which the municipal government had to borrow from other industries. It is now heard that 15,000 yuan of the 25,000 yuan that was borrowed from other industries has been obtained as of the other day, leaving a shortfall of 10,000 yuan, which Mayor Yang has entrusted to Chairman Lin Qinxiang of the General Chamber of Commerce to borrow from the pharmacy industry. If this can be achieved, then after the contract is signed, it can be established. It is heard that the short-term construction public bonds that were previously collateralized by the wharf donation and the new 40,000 yuan loan that was collateralized by the vehicle donation must be deducted. In this way, the actual amount obtained by the municipal government is still a drop in the bucket and does not help the situation. As for the members of the Management Committee, Mayor Yang still insists on retaining them all without reappointing them, in order to benefit from their experience.

No One Bids for the City's Sutra and Repentance Donation The Ningbo City's sutra and repentance donation was originally scheduled to be bid on the 15th of this month at the Finance Bureau of the Municipal Government. It is heard that as of yesterday, there were still no bidders. This is probably due to the impact of the central government's order to abolish the sutra and repentance donation in various provinces, cities, and counties. According to the various sections of the Finance Bureau, this sutra and repentance donation is included in the municipal education fund. If it is abolished now, the education fund will be short again, and it must be remedied in another way.

The Yuyao Chief Prosecutor's Malfeasance Case Will Be Tried Separately The case of Yang Hongjun, the chief prosecutor of the Yuyao County Court, being accused of malfeasance has been transferred by the High Court to the Yin County Local Court for trial. The court has repeatedly opened hearings and summoned witnesses. There is a co-defendant in the case, Wang Zaichen, the deputy director of the Yuyao China Bank. After the previous trial, he was temporarily released on bail with a guarantee from Wang Yingzhou, who was acting on behalf of Lu. Unexpectedly, Wang Zaichen returned to Yao for medical treatment due to illness. He failed to appear at the previous summons. The prosecutor was furious and immediately arrested Wang Yingzhou and Lu and ordered them to hand over Wang Zaichen. It is now found that Wang Zaichen came to Yong yesterday afternoon to surrender. After being questioned by the prosecutor, he was released on bail for 1,000 yuan in cash at the request of a certain cigarette shop. The guarantors Wang Yingzhou and Lu, who had been arrested, were also released immediately. Yang Hongjun had previously changed his guarantor to a certain cigarette paper shop because the original guarantor had withdrawn.

Another Bandit Robbery in the Southern Countryside of Yuyao About twenty miles from Yuyao County City, there is a resident named Lv Chunyang in Tongde Township's Liushuitan Village, who earns his living by farming and manages his family diligently, so he has accumulated some savings over the years. This has aroused the covetousness of some bandits. Unexpectedly, in the third watch of the night before last, more than ten robbers suddenly came, wearing blue cloth short shirts and holding shell guns and other weapons, breaking down the door and entering the room, forbidding any outcry. Fortunately, the old and young in Yangchun's family knew there was something wrong when they heard the door knocking, and escaped through the back door, avoiding harm. However, all the belongings and the cash in the house were looted. Afterwards, the bandits all fled south. The estimated losses are over 600 yuan.

Shaoxing

Time Limit for Demolition and Concession of Streets: Magistrate Tang, in order to facilitate transportation, previously ordered the demolition and concession of streets from Dajiang Bridge to Qingdao Bridge to facilitate road construction. Due to requests from the business community for an extension, meetings were held to discuss the matter, and it was submitted to the Provincial Department of Construction for approval. Instructions have now been received, stipulating the method of demolition and concession: Dajiang Bridge to Qingdao Bridge is divided into two sections, Beihai Slope to Shuicheng Bridge into two sections, and Qingdao Bridge to Wuyunmen into three sections. Each section has a time limit of three months for completion of the demolition and concession.

Handling the Distribution of Low-Priced Rice: The county government has issued a notice to organize committees in all rural areas of the county to implement the plan for selling rice at low prices. Yesterday, the Food Maintenance Association distributed the rice according to the plan. In addition to allocating 3,000 bags of unpolished rice to the disaster areas of Tianle, Dezheng, and Xialu Townships, the allocations were: 1,691 bags for District 1, 1,000 bags for District 2, 670 bags for District 3, 400 bags for District 4, 740 bags for District 5, 860 bags for District 6, 440 bags for District 7, 1,500 bags for District 8, 1,700 bags for District 9, and 950 bags for District 10. The price of polished rice is set at 14 yuan per stone, and unpolished rice at 12 yuan per stone. Based on the county's population of 1,123,274, each person will receive approximately nine 合 of rice per day. The sale will be completed within 20 days from the start date.

False Alarm at the Prison: At 4:00 PM on the 17th, there was a rumor of a riot by prisoners at the Shaoxing Prison. Military police from various locations rushed to provide security. However, upon arrival, no such activity was found. Because Warden Yang was out, cunning prisoners fabricated the rumor in hopes of being released.

Over a Thousand Tenant Farmers Gather at the County to Petition: At approximately 2:00 PM on the 12th, over one thousand farmers from Nanhutian Village in the Fourth Northern Township sent representatives Chen Zhaohua, Gu Junhui, Yu Guosheng, and Lian Guangjie to the County Government, County Party Headquarters, and Agricultural Consolidation Committee to petition. The purpose of their request was generally as follows: The rice they planted is now mature and ready for harvest. Last year, the estimation of the total harvest was delayed, resulting in an extremely lean year. The estimated yield was more than four stone per mu. However, the landlords were even more greedy, with some seeking to pursue legal action against the farmers. The people have already suffered from the disaster, and now they are burdened by lawsuits. Now that the rice is about to ripen, they fear repeating last year's situation. They propose suspending the harvesting of all rice in Nanhutian, requesting a quick estimation of the yield, and asking for the clear definition of a "public dou" measure to avoid disputes. After the main personnel of each agency met with them, the main points of their response can be divided into three points: (1) The harvest yield can be estimated jointly by the local township office or the district party branch in accordance with the regulations. (2) The amount of rent needs to be requested from the provincial authorities for further instructions. (3) The "public dou" measure will continue to be issued by the province as the standard and promulgated. The representatives were satisfied and gradually dispersed.

Xiaoshan

Statistics on the Area of Farmland in Xiaoshan County: Statistics on the area of farmland in Xiaoshan County, obtained through a survey by the Statistics Department of the Legislative Yuan, are divided into five categories: (1) Total area of farmland: 1,096,185 mu. (2) Area of paddy fields: 559,054 mu. (3) Area of dry land on plains: 482,322 mu. (4) Area of dry land on hillsides: 54,809 mu. (5) Area of cultivable but uncultivated land: 100,000 mu.

Tea, Wine, and Vegetable Tax Subsidizes Police Salaries: The 49th Xiaoshan County Government meeting formulated draft regulations for taxes on teahouses, wine shops, and restaurants, deciding to change the name to "Subsidies for Police Salaries." Monthly taxes will be collected from teahouses, wine shops, and restaurants, and separate measures for collecting the subsidies will be formulated. The tax rates are divided into: Special grade: 4 to 10 yuan per month; First grade: 2 yuan; Second grade: 1 yuan; Third grade: 5 jiao. The Director of the Finance Bureau and the Section Chief will be appointed to jointly formulate the collection measures.
