Yu Qiaqing's Great Act of Relieving People's Food Shortage

Jointly Purchasing 100,000 Stones of Foreign Rice for Sale at Cost

Mr. Yu Qiaqing, seeing that rice prices are soaring and the people are struggling to obtain food, believes that if efforts are not made to provide relief, the poor will have no rice to cook. Therefore, he has contacted the Ministry of Finance, Shanghai Municipal Government, Public Concession Authorities, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, proposing to jointly purchase 100,000 stones of foreign rice for sale at cost to relieve the people's food shortage. The Ministry of Finance and the Municipal Government have already agreed. In the Public Concession, Mr. Yu and the other four Chinese Directors have written a letter to the Chairman of the Board of Directors, Mr. Magnaunton, who has also agreed. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce is still discussing the matter. In addition, the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association has sent a letter to the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association, requesting them to forward it to the five Chinese Directors Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Zhu Yanzi, Wei Tingrong, and Lu Bohong, asking them to consult with the French Concession Public Board of Directors to participate and work together to achieve this good deed and achieve significant results.

Municipal Government Sets Deadline for Zoning

To Be Completed Within 20 Days of Receiving the Notice

The New Municipal Organization Law was promulgated by the Government on May 20th of this year. Article 5 stipulates that the city shall be divided into districts, neighborhoods, 里 and 鄰. Except in special circumstances, a 鄰 shall consist of five households, a 里 shall consist of five 鄰, a 坊 shall consist of twenty 里, and a 區 shall consist of ten 坊. Article 139 stipulates that the Municipal Government shall, within three months after the implementation of this law, divide the city into several districts, neighborhoods, 里 and 鄰, and report them to the superior authorities separately. According to these regulations, each city shall complete the zoning within three months after the implementation of the New Law. The Shanghai Municipal Government, facing a tight deadline, is proceeding without delay. In addition to appointing committee members to form a preparatory committee for the implementation of the Municipal Organization Law to ensure progress, it also issued orders to the municipal committee members of each district yesterday, instructing them to promptly and accurately fill out the forms and complete the work within 20 days of receiving the notice, without further delay.

French Business Water and Electricity Workers' Strike Expands

Vehicle Department Supports the Strike

Support Committee to Meet Today

Details of the French Business Water and Electricity Workers' Union strike have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that workers in the Vehicle Department are also suffering from oppression by the capitalists. Seeing the enthusiastic struggle of the workers in the Machine Department, they spontaneously joined the strike committee yesterday morning, signing their names to express their cooperation and willingness to unite in the fight against the imperialist capitalists. By the afternoon, over 200 people had registered. A few drivers have not expressed their sympathy, but most have left. The union is now trying to persuade them to participate in the strike movement as a whole.

Union Holds a General Meeting: After the Vehicle Department expressed its support, the union convened a general meeting of all workers at 3:00 PM yesterday at the Public Stadium. Over 800 workers, including those from the Vehicle Department, attended. Xu Yefu was sent by the Municipal Party Headquarters to attend, and the Second District Police Station of the Public Security Bureau sent police to maintain order at the meeting. Chairman Xu Amei reported on the situation of the Vehicle Department workers joining the strike, expressing the hope that everyone would unite to deal with the capitalists, so that it would not be difficult to win the final victory. Subsequently, Xu Yefu gave instructions, followed by Zhang Amao reporting on recent union affairs, and finally, Shen Kemin, the representative of the Vehicle Department, gave a speech expressing the meaning of support.

Support Committee Holds a Meeting: The establishment of the Shanghai Municipal All-Union Support Committee for the French Business Water and Electricity Workers' Union has been reported in previous issues. It is now learned that the committee has established an office in the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union and will hold its first meeting at 10:00 AM today to implement the decisions of the general meeting and discuss support measures to actively proceed.

Three Workers Arrested: Yesterday, three more striking workers from the Machine Department were arrested by the French police. It is said that the workers were not acting out of line when they were arrested.

French Police Take Strict Precautions: Yesterday afternoon, the French Concession Police Station issued an order to the head of each police station under its jurisdiction to immediately send armed detectives to the areas bordering the Chinese and French concessions, such as Min Guo Road, Nanyang Bridge, Fangbang Bridge, Xie Bridge, Shiliupu, and Xiaodongmen, to strengthen security. In addition, the iron gates in various places were temporarily closed, leaving only the side doors on the pedestrian walkways open for pedestrians to pass through. Only two iron gates at the intersection of Dongxin Bridge Street and Min Guo Road were left open for vehicles to pass through.

Another Tram in the French Concession Attacked Yesterday

At 9:50 AM yesterday, a crowd of people resembling workers suddenly gathered at the intersection of Xujiahui Road and Caishi Road in the French Concession. At that time, French Business Tram No. 164 on Route 18 was passing by. The crowd took out stones and smashed more than half of the windows of the tram. By the time the detectives arrived, the crowd had scattered and fled. Upon hearing the news, the police authorities, noting that there have been frequent incidents of vandalism against trams recently, specifically ordered a large number of detectives to be stationed at tram stops and along the main roads through which trams pass. At the same time, hundreds of volunteers wearing armbands with the French tricolor flag patrolled everywhere to provide security. It is reported that the French Business Tram Company authorities believe that if necessary, they will temporarily suspend tram services to avoid any crisis and unnecessary sacrifices.

Shanghai-Japan Submarine Cable Interrupted Yesterday Morning

Must Be Relayed Through Guam

The Da Wan Bao newspaper reports that the direct submarine cable to Japan from this port has been interrupted due to a severe hurricane whose center passed 70 miles southwest of Nagasaki this morning (18th), causing turbulent waves at sea. Therefore, it is no longer possible to send telegrams. All telegrams to Japan must be relayed through Guam until the cable is repaired, which will inevitably cause delays.

Price Reduction for News Telegrams to Europe

Effective August 1st

Reuters Shanghai, 18th: According to the agreement between the local telegraph office and various submarine cable companies, the cost of news telegrams to Europe will be reduced from 1.25 gold francs to 0.86 gold francs, effective August 1st. At the current exchange rate, this is equivalent to 6 jiao 7 fen in Chinese currency.

Both Railways Temporarily Suspend the Sale of Through Tickets on the Jinpu Railway

The Traffic Department of the Jinghu-Hangyong Railway Administration telegraphed the station staff of both railways yesterday, stating: "Due to the lack of vehicles on the Jinpu Railway, the sale of through tickets on both railways and the Jinpu Railway will be temporarily suspended from yesterday (18th). However, tickets from Hangzhou and Shanghai stations will only be sold to Nanjing. Please take note."

Domestic Public Debt Maintenance Association Cables to Maintain Public Debt

(1) Cable to the National Government: To the National Government in Nanjing, we note with concern the recent sharp decline in public debt, creating a dangerous situation, undermining national credit, and leading to economic bankruptcy. Please immediately cable the Central Bank and the Bank of Communications to ensure that bonds used as collateral or for discount that are repaying principal and interest on schedule are treated equally without exception, and that excuses not be used to reject such bonds so as to undermine bond credibility. Also instruct the Ministry of Finance to order the Director General of Customs to announce the precise amount of revenue and expenditure from the funds each ten days to clarify the truth and dispel rumors. Furthermore, inform the Shanghai Securities Exchange that all those selling futures must first deposit the goods as collateral, without needing to deposit a separate security deposit, and that those who do not first deposit the goods should not be allowed to sell short, thereby preventing the abuses of speculation, manipulation, and the fabrication of rumors to depress prices. This is a fundamental relief measure. We respectfully request that this be promptly submitted to the State Council for discussion and maintenance, so as to ensure bond credibility and maintain the economy. The Shanghai Domestic Public Debt Maintenance Association.

(2) Cable to the Ministry of Finance: To the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, the price of public debt has been declining gradually and sharply in recent months, and the customs bonds have declined to little over 3000 yuan per 10,000, and the military reorganization bonds have declined to a little over 3000 yuan per 10,000, and other bonds have also declined in value. The national economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the foundation of the banks is dangerously shaky. If remedies are not sought urgently, the dangerous situation may give rise to irretrievable outcomes. Viewing the crisis, we could not stand by idly and do nothing, so we are sending you a cable respectfully requesting that your department instruct the Director General of Customs and the Committee for the Management of the Customs 25 Treasury Bond Fund to publish the revenue and expenditure of the public debt fund in newspapers every ten days in a clear announcement, and that you allow representatives to be sent from the Silver Trade Association and the Market Traders' Association to go and conduct an inspection and confirm, so that the people of the country may know that your department has not been using the public debt fund, thereby dispelling doubts and stopping rumors. Furthermore, we request that you order the Central Bank and the Bank of Communications to treat bonds used as collateral and for discount that are repaying principal and interest on a monthly basis that are not behind schedule equally and without exception, and not to make excuses or reject them, so as to avoid damaging bond credibility. Banks that have been specially permitted by the government to issue banknotes must also handle it the same way, and those who resist or refuse should be regarded as undermining bond credibility and be subject to legal sanctions. Furthermore, the Shanghai Securities Exchange should be ordered to notify all brokers that all those selling futures must first deposit the goods as collateral, and that the usual security deposit does not need to be paid again, and that all those who do not have the goods at hand who intend to speculate by selling short should be rejected, and that your department should send a staff member to be stationed specially in the Securities Exchange to inspect the depositing of the goods so as to verify the conclusion of transactions, so that generally those who fabricate rumors of unsuccessful military operations to lower the market price and profit by selling short will have no place to implement their tricks. This is a fundamental relief measure, and we ask you to make a prompt and decisive decision and be responsible for its implementation, so as to maintain bond credibility and maintain the economy. The Shanghai Domestic Public Debt Maintenance Association.

Women's Comfort Goods Transported to Beijing

The loading area at the North Station was very crowded last night because there were many items urgently needing to be loaded. Among them, the most noticeable were over 33,000 pairs of straw sandals, over 30,000 cans each of candy and preserved vegetables, over 60,000 towels, 135 boxes of braised bamboo shoots, and 30 boxes of medicinal liquid. Minutes of the Executive Committee Standing Meeting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Appendix: Meeting Rules

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce held an Executive Committee Standing Meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday. Executive Committee members Wang Yansong, Fang Jiaobo, Luo Qinghua, Yuan Ludeng, Lu Fengzhu, Wu Zhihao, Lu Wenshao, and Ye Huijun, and more than ten other people attended. Yuan Ludeng was publicly elected as chairman. The resolutions are recorded below: (1) The Chamber's meeting rules were discussed, modified, and passed. (2) The simplified rules for the establishment of branch offices by various trade associations were discussed, modified, and passed, and will be submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval. (3) On the matter of how to respond to foreigners invading Shanghai's western district, building roads beyond the boundaries, and controlling police power, it was resolved: (1) To issue a declaration opposing foreigners' invasion of our country's police power. (2) To request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to quickly recover the roads built beyond the boundaries. (3) To request the Municipal Government to argue based on reason and insist to the end. (4) To send a letter to the Chinese Directors to argue based on reason. (5) To urge the Chinese Ratepayers Association to immediately convene an Executive Committee meeting to work together to strive for a resolution. The meeting adjourned. The meeting rules of the Chamber are recorded as follows:

Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Meeting Rules Article 1. These rules are formulated in accordance with Chapter 8 of the Chamber's charter. Article 2. The types of meetings are as follows: (1) General Meeting of Members: Held regularly in mid-June each year, convened by the Executive Committee. (2) Executive Committee: Holds two regular meetings per month, held on the first and third Fridays of each month, convened by the Standing Committee. (3) Supervisory Committee: Holds one regular meeting per month, held on the third Friday of each month. (4) Standing Committee: Holds one regular meeting per week, held every Thursday. (5) Various Stock Committees: Hold at least one meeting per month, the date to be determined temporarily by each Stock Committee. Article 3. The General Meeting of Members may be convened as a special meeting when the Executive Committee deems it necessary, or when requested by more than one-tenth of the member representatives, or when the Supervisory Committee sends a letter requesting a meeting. Article 4. The Executive Committee may convene a special meeting when the Standing Committee deems it necessary, or when proposed by three or more committee members. Article 5. When the General Meeting of Members is held, a resolution can only be made if more than half of the member representatives are present and more than half of the attending representatives agree. If the number of attending representatives is less than half, a provisional resolution can be made, and the results will be notified to each representative. The General Meeting of Members will be reconvened one week later, within two weeks, and the provisional resolution will be enacted if more than half of those attending agree. Article 6. A resolution on the following matters shall be made with the agreement of more than two-thirds of the attending representatives, with more than two-thirds of the member representatives present. If the number of attending representatives exceeds half but is less than two-thirds, a provisional resolution may be passed with the agreement of more than two-thirds of the attending representatives, and the results will be notified to each representative. The General Meeting of Members will be reconvened one week later, within two weeks, and the provisional resolution will be enacted if more than two-thirds of those attending agree: (1) Amending the charter; (2) Expelling members or member representatives; (3) Resigning staff members; (4) Appointing liquidators and resolving matters related to liquidation; (5) Resolving matters related to the issuance of public bonds.

###

###

Page 14

Article 7. When the Executive Committee, Supervisory Committee, Standing Committee, or Stock Committee is in session, there must be more than half of the committee members present, and a resolution can only be made with the agreement of more than half of the attending committee members. If the number of votes for and against is the same, the chairman shall decide. Article 8. When the General Meeting of Members is in session, the Standing Committee shall organize a presidium to take turns chairing the meeting. Article 9. When the Executive Committee and the Standing Committee are in session, the chairman of the committee shall chair the meeting. If the chairman is absent, the committee members shall publicly elect one person to be the chairman. Article 10. When the Supervisory Committee is in session, they shall temporarily elect one person to be the chairman. Article 11. Supervisory Committee members may attend the Executive Committee, have the right to speak, but do not have the right to vote. Article 12. Meeting proposals must be sent to the meeting three days in advance and included in the agenda. Temporary motions or changes to the agenda must have a second before they can be discussed. Article 13. During the meeting, if a committee member or member is unable to attend, they must request leave before the meeting and may also entrust another committee member or member representative with a letter of proxy, but one person cannot represent two people, except in the case of elections. Article 14. If a motion is deemed to require review, a review committee may be temporarily elected to review it. Article 15. Committee members may not leave the meeting without good reason. If there is an unavoidable accident and it is necessary to leave, the reason must be stated and the chairman's permission must be obtained before leaving. Article 16. If a meeting is about a matter concerning a committee member or member, they may be ordered to temporarily leave the meeting. Article 17. When making a statement, one must stand up, first call on the chairman to request the right to speak. Article 18. During the meeting, one must wait for Party A to finish speaking before Party B can stand up again. Article 19. Except for those who have been invited or specifically permitted to attend, no one is allowed to listen in on the meeting. Article 20. The minutes of the meeting shall be read aloud on the spot at the next meeting, and after being acknowledged or revised, they shall be signed by the chairman. Article 21. These rules shall apply to all meetings of the Chamber. Article 22. If there are any matters not covered by these rules, they shall be handled in accordance with the People's Rights Preliminary. Article 21. These rules shall be implemented after being passed by the Executive Committee and shall be revised in the same way.

Achievements of the Jianghai Customs in Seizing Prohibited Items such as Opium and Morphine

According to the report of the Jianghai Customs Commissioner, the number of prohibited items such as opium and morphine seized in April, May, and June of the 19th year is as follows: a total of 68,132 taels of foreign and domestic opium, estimated value of silver dollars 160,813.15; 8 dan and 74 jin of poppy flowers, estimated value of silver dollars 131.10; 201 taels of heroin, estimated value of silver dollars 7,537.50; and various drugs containing toxic substances, estimated value of silver dollars 729.50.

Cash Exports to Japan Transferred Through Dalian

Consul General in Kobe Cables Requesting Attention

Since the gold is expensive and silver is cheap incident, unscrupulous merchants have been secretly transporting cash abroad in order to make huge profits. The huge amount of gold bars seized on the Canadian ship the other day is concrete evidence of this. Lu Zhaokun, our country's Consul General in Kobe, Japan, sent letters to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and a certain important person in this port separately yesterday, requesting that the Jianghai Customs be consulted to pay close attention to and search ships sailing from Shanghai to Dalian, because gold bars being transported to Japan are now mostly relayed through Dalian.

Changes in Silver Holdings in this Port

One Increase and One Decrease

According to investigations yesterday, the export of silver dollars from this port has been quite large this week, so the decrease is also significant, but silver bullion has suddenly increased. In real terms, silver dollars decreased by 935,000 taels, while silver bullion increased by 560,000 taels.

The 161st Meeting

On July 4th, the Municipal Government held its 161st municipal conference. (2) According to the order from the Central Party Headquarters regarding the remission of deducted salaries, the money has now been returned. All income tax that was exempted during the deduction period should be paid. The Municipal Government will comply with this and has already issued a notice to all bureaus. 2. The "Provisional Regulations for the Management of Veterinarians in the Shanghai Special Municipality" was discussed. The proposal concerning the Shanghai Municipal Council's plan to build a new bridge on Hongqiao Road and the need for consultation on the appropriate response was discussed. It was resolved that the Shanghai Municipal Council should be allowed to request approval for the construction in accordance with the "Regulations on the Construction of Roads, Bridges, Wharves, and Revetments at the request of Citizens of Shanghai Municipality."

Record of the Shanghai County District Administration Meeting

The Shanghai County Government held its fourth district administration meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Attendees included the heads of various districts, as well as Ye Dezhen and Yu Fen, section chiefs from the County Government Secretariat. County Magistrate Yan presided over the meeting, with Hu Gongshou as the recorder. After the formalities were duly observed, the following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding the order from the Department of Civil Affairs to complete and report on citizen oath registration and township elections within the shortest possible timeframe, a discussion was held on when this should be completed. It was resolved that citizen oath registration should be completed by the end of August, and township elections would be scheduled immediately after the registration is completed. (2) Regarding whether there is a need to re-establish township preparatory offices, a discussion was held. It was resolved that the current township offices in each district will serve as the preparatory offices for the future official township offices. (3) Regarding the urgent requests from the provincial department concerning personnel registration, a discussion was held on the need to set a deadline for submitting the first month's registration summary to the county for verification. It was resolved that the registration situation and registration summary for June should be submitted to the county by the end of July, and all subsequent submissions must be submitted monthly. (4) Regarding how to guide and promote farmers' cooperative societies, a discussion was held. It was resolved that each district should actively promote and proceed in accordance with the cooperative society regulations. (5) Regarding the proposal by the first district head concerning township heads acting as agents for busy transport and the request for an allocation of collection fees to emphasize responsibility, the matter was previously submitted but has not been convened for a month. A request was made to order the Finance Bureau to convene and resolve the matter promptly. It was resolved to forward the matter to the Finance Bureau.

"Yuan Da" Steamer Detained by Soviet Russian Fleet

The local Yi Da Steamship Company owns a steamer called "Yuan Da," which can carry more than 6,300 tons and is the largest ship owned by Chinese people in recent times. In March of this year, it was leased to the Vladivostok Soviet Russian Commercial Fleet for operation, with a monthly rental of $15,000. Unexpectedly, when the ship was sailing back to Vladivostok from Tokyo in early April, it hit a reef due to fog about ten miles from Vladivostok. The Soviet Russian fleet dispatched ships to rescue it, including two icebreakers and one barge. First, the cargo in the ship was unloaded, and then the "Yuan Da" was towed back to Vladivostok. Vladivostok's shipyard, the only one in the city, is state-owned by Soviet Russia. The shipyard refused to repair it but agreed to provide temporary emergency repairs to make it seaworthy for one voyage so that it could be formally repaired in another port. These temporary repairs would cost 11,000 gold rubles, equivalent to about $20,000 in Chinese currency. However, since the accident, the Soviet Russian fleet has telegraphed to declare the termination of the lease and to stop paying rent. According to international practice, anyone who provides assistance when a ship has an accident at sea should receive a salvage fee. This salvage fee should be borne by the shipowner and the cargo owners in proportion to the value of the ship and the cargo. This is the so-called general average. After receiving the news of the "Yuan Da" hitting the reef, the local Yi Da Company sent Nao Cheng, a Chinese shipowner named Pu Li, to Vladivostok to represent the company and handle various matters concerning the ship. After Pu Li arrived in Vladivostok, he repeatedly consulted with the managers of the Soviet Russian fleet, requesting that they announce the total value of the cargo, quickly determine the amount of salvage costs, and assess the value of the "Yuan Da" in order to calculate the salvage costs to be borne by the ship. Although the temporary repairs had been completed, the Soviet Russian fleet delayed fulfilling the above assessment and other matters. Since the lease had been terminated, all losses from the monthly $15,000 rental were borne by the shipowner. After repeated urgings by Yi Da's representative, shipowner Pu Li, they continued to make excuses. Finally, one week after the incident, on May 27th, they sent a letter to the representative requesting the shipowner to deposit 80,000 Japanese yen (equivalent to more than $160,000 in Chinese currency) to release the ship to be repaired in another port. Pu Li replied, asking how this amount was calculated, but after several inquiries, there was no response. The total value of the cargo on board was never disclosed. Pu Li went to the fleet's office and protested verbally, asking how much the ship was valued at. At first, they said 97,000 gold rubles. Later, when Pu Li questioned why the salvage cost was more than 80% of the estimated value, creating an unprecedented example in the world for calculating salvage costs, they deliberately raised the ship's price to 120,000 to 180,000 gold rubles. When asked how much the cargo on board was worth, they said that there were two bills of lading, each worth about $40,000 US dollars, with an approximate total value of 300,000 Japanese yen. However, they were only expressed verbally and were not willing to put them in writing. Pu Li requested to see various supporting documents, but they were all rejected. After many negotiations in Vladivostok without any effect, he returned to Shanghai in anger and reported the details of the negotiations to Yi Da Company. The company consulted various well-known shipping experts in Shanghai on the matter. According to the experts' opinions, icebreakers are government property of Soviet Russia. According to international maritime law, in addition to actual expenses, no salvage remuneration can be requested. The actual expenses required for the rescue must be very limited. Even if it is still paid according to ordinary salvage remuneration, the maximum should not exceed 80,000 Japanese yen. However, this refers to the total salvage cost for the ship and cargo. According to the fleet's initial estimate of the ship's price, the shipowner's share should be at most one-quarter of the total salvage cost. The demand for 80,000 Japanese yen to release the ship is not known on what basis. Now the shipowner Yi Da Company has entrusted the local lawyer Cai Rudong to handle the matter on its behalf. The reporter of the Guowen News Agency visited lawyer Cai the day before yesterday. According to Cai, in order to attempt a reconciliation, he has telegraphed the Vladivostok Soviet Russian Commercial Fleet that the shipowner here is willing to deposit 25,000 Japanese yen in the bank to urge them to release the ship immediately. Otherwise, our responsibility has been exhausted, and we have been particularly generous in calculating the salvage costs, making excessive concessions. If the Soviet Russian fleet persists in its error, the shipowner will have appropriate countermeasures. Under the red imperialism, even if the shipowner cannot obtain fair treatment, the "Yuan Da" ship lease contract stipulates that the place for delivery and return of the ship, payment of rent, and adjudication of disputes is Shanghai. Since the place for fulfilling the contractual obligations has been clearly specified in Shanghai, the Chinese court has jurisdiction over the case according to law. When service is made in the future, it can be executed in accordance with the Civil Procedure Regulations, and any property of the fleet in China can be seized to compensate the shipowner's losses. According to lawyer's opinion, the fleet's request for 80,000 Japanese yen to release the ship is ridiculous. In addition to 80,000 Japanese yen, the shipowner must also pay 11,000 gold rubles for temporary repairs. In the future, formal repairs will require another 40,000 to 50,000 taels of silver. If so, the ship will cost a total of 240,000 to 250,000 Chinese dollars. The ship is not actually worth this amount, and the suspension of navigation for four months at a loss of 15,000 yuan per month totals 60,000 yuan, not to mention other expenses. The fleet's behavior is intended to confiscate the ship by taking the opportunity. How can the shipowner willingly submit and tolerate such a large loss? Therefore, he has decided to do everything possible to deal with it. As for the shipowner's inherent rights, he will never give up even a thread of loss. It is learned that many ships operating under the Soviet Russian fleet are leased from Chinese ship merchants. After the "Yuan Da" accident, the fleet has adopted such a strong and unreasonable attitude. In the future, Chinese shipping merchants who lease ships to the fleet should also be aware of the precautions. Even more, the ship lease contract stipulates that British law applies. In the long history of Britain, the salvage fee obtained by rescuers has never exceeded 50% of the value of the rescued object, and this ratio can only be obtained if the ship has already been abandoned. Now, the "Yuan Da" is only aground on the bow, and the fleet dispatched ships to provide some assistance and towed it to Vladivostok, but it is taking the opportunity to extort money and attempt to confiscate the shipowner's ship. Not only have the local shipping experts never heard of it, but it is indeed a matter that should be noted by countries around the world.

Native Cloth Exempt from Parcel Tax

The local Parcel Tax Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Finance yesterday stating that native cloth is related to the prosperity or decline of domestic goods. Moreover, at a time when the National Government is promoting domestic goods, the parcel tax on native cloth should be exempted across the board to relieve commercial difficulties and conform to the original intention of promotion.

Changbang Rice Merchants Did Not Collect Special Donations

The Shanghai Changshu Rice Merchants Association previously had a rumor of major activities to collect special donations from various shipowners in the group. After receiving the report, the Social Affairs Bureau detained Jin Kai, an employee of the association, and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for custody and interrogation. It was previously reported that Jin Kai confessed that the collection of special donations was decided by the executive and supervisory meetings of the association and had nothing to do with him. Jin Kai was allowed to be released on bail, and the Social Affairs Bureau ordered the Changshu Rice Merchants Association to clearly respond to the reasons for collecting special donations. According to the reply, the collection of special donations was purely proposed by a few shipowners. The executive committee decided to retain the matter in the minutes of the meeting because it involved increasing the burden on members, which can be used as evidence. Unexpectedly, Jin Kai spread rumors outside that the executive committee had decided to collect donations, thinking of profiting from it. Lu Junwen found out the truth and immediately notified the shipowners, which did not become a reality. After inquiring with the shipowners in Shanghai, they said that they had not paid special donations. The rumors are purely fabricated. Please exempt Lu Junwen from investigation, etc. Since the Social Affairs Bureau confirmed that special donations were not actually collected, the situation is still forgivable. However, Lu Junwen repeatedly resisted summons and did not arrive, which is really inappropriate. Since he has not participated in this matter, he should still go to the bureau for inquiries. The association is responsible for dredging the source and supervising the rice merchants to strictly abide by government orders and provide a guarantee to the bureau to avoid further investigation.

Evaluation Method Agreed Upon for Registration

The Shanghai Rice Milling Industry Association held an executive committee meeting the day before yesterday. More than a dozen members attended, including Lu Guishan, Pan Xianting, Zhu Zixiang, and Liu Wenhao. Chairman Zhu Zixiang reported briefly that, according to Instruction No. 2535 from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the white rice of the North City factories and warehouses must be registered and evaluated in accordance with the white rice of the He Xia, and must not be sold without authorization. After discussion, all agreed that the industry currently has very little inventory, only enough for retail sales at the door. If there is indeed surplus inventory and they want to sell it, they should strictly abide by the instruction, register directly with the Rice Merchants Association, and openly evaluate it. However, they must follow the pure method of the South City and sell it through the Rice Merchants. As for the warehouse goods, it is not within the scope of the association, so it is not convenient to plan on their behalf. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Long-Silent Case of the Grand Light

Scheduled to Open in Court This Month on the 24th in the Afternoon

The Grand Light Cinema showed the sound film "Not Afraid of Death" in March of this year. Hong Shen, a teacher at Fudan University, went to see it and found that the content of the film was too insulting to Chinese people. He immediately gave a speech. The audience was moved by Hong, and most of them left. The manager of the cinema, Gao Yongqing, called the police and arrested Hong and detained him in the New Gate Police Station. After negotiations, he was released. Hong submitted a report to the Municipal Party Department and forwarded it to the Central Government, ordering the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with the US government, and filed a complaint against Gao in the former Provisional Court. The trial was opened once, but it was postponed due to the hope of a settlement. Counting the fingers, it has been almost four months, and the news of the settlement has been extremely silent, and it is expected to be hopeless. Last month, the plaintiff, Hong Shen, believed that the case had been delayed for too long, which was not right, so he hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to request the Special District District Court to schedule a trial as soon as possible. It is now learned that the court has scheduled the case to be heard this month on the 24th at 2:00 PM. Yesterday, the police officers sent notices to the plaintiff's lawyers, Zhan Jifeng and Wu Chengyu, and the defendant's lawyers, Jiang Baoli, to inform the parties concerned that they must appear in court on time and await trial.

The Hurricane Did Not Reach Shanghai

It Has Reached the Waters off Nagasaki, Japan

The second hurricane discovered over the Pacific Ocean has now entered the inland sea. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, according to a report from the Yangjingbang Observatory, it has blown to 131 degrees east longitude and 33 degrees north latitude, in the waters off Nagasaki, Japan, and is spreading widely. The wind is trending northeast and north, and it seems that it will land. From this point of view, the saying that Shanghai will have a second hurricane may no longer become a reality.

A Mad Woman Who Killed Two People Declared Not Guilty

Not Responsible for Anything When Insane

Should Regain Freedom Once the Madness Has Healed

Jiang Xu, a woman from Wuxi, suffered from mental illness. After being treated in the New Universal Charity Asylum for the Insane, she was discharged after she recovered. Later, she suffered from other diseases and was sent to the Sanatorium Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, her madness relapsed and she took a kitchen knife and killed two women who were being treated in the same hospital. She was immediately sent back to the Asylum for the Insane for treatment and has since recovered. After examining the deceased, the prosecutor of the local court filed a public prosecution in accordance with the law. After the debate was opened, she claimed that at that time she only felt blurred vision. In her eyes, she saw two black fish and had been drooling with anticipation for eggplant for a long time. So she took a kitchen knife in the hospital to kill the fish, but they were people. It was the ghost's fault, not mine. The judge announced the end of the trial. Yesterday, Judge Zhao ordered Jiang Xu to be brought to the court to announce the verdict: Jiang Xu was found not guilty and should be allowed to be free. The reason for the verdict was that the woman was originally insane and mentally lost. This was due to the hospital's negligence in preventing it. After her illness was diagnosed, she should have known that her freedom should not have been restricted. Moreover, the hospital setting up kitchen knives was also negligent. Therefore, the fault was not with the defendant, and she should not be held criminally liable. She was therefore advised to be not guilty. As for the defendant who has now been cured, she must no longer be bound by her freedom and should be allowed to be free. After the verdict, the woman was returned to the prosecutor's office and sent to the New Universal Charity Asylum for collection.

Casia Requests the Return of Confiscated Property

Requests All Items Except Gambling Equipment to be Returned

Casia, the principal offender in the roulette gambling den case at 151 Jingan Temple Road, has now been released after serving his sentence and is presenting a petition to the Special District District Court to request the return of all confiscated property except gambling equipment. This petition was originally intended to be delivered to the court yesterday, but it was changed to today because there were still corrections to be made. It is heard that this past Tuesday, Casia was allowed by the court to go to the archives with a lawyer to review the files of the case and investigate the confiscated items.

Discovery in Pudong

Superstition Tax Collection Agency

One Agency Splitting into Two

Pudong Even Manages Nanshi

Seized False Letters of Appointment, etc.

Zhang Youshi May Have Been Deceived

Yesterday, detectives from the Third District of the Public Security Bureau discovered a cunning agency claiming to collect superstition taxes on Huayuan Shiqiao Main Street, Pudong. Various false documents were seized. The details are recorded as follows: The agency is small but very busy. In February of this year, a long strip of white paper suddenly appeared at the entrance of a building at No. 151 Huayuan Shiqiao Main Street, north of Lan Ni Du, Pudong, reading "Shanghai Special Municipality Finance Bureau Pudong Superstition Tax Collection Branch Preparatory Office." Many people, both men and women, entered and exited every day. Passersby often stopped to watch. The interior was quite neatly arranged, resembling a small-scale agency. The staff inside seemed to be very busy. Recently, a piece of paper with the words "Nanshi Collection Office" was added to the entrance, splitting one agency into two. Those who didn't know suspected it was a development of their work. Unexpectedly, the fate of the agency ended at this time. The Finance Bureau was always unaware. District Chief Zhang of the Third District reported to the General Bureau for investigation because the agency was very eye-catching. Director Yuan was also suspicious because he had not received a formal notice from the Finance Bureau. He immediately inquired with the Finance Bureau, which also denied appointing anyone to set up an agency in Pudong to collect superstition taxes. Therefore, he instructed Shen Tong, the Shanghai South Director of the bureau, to send two investigators, Cheng Yushu and Cheng Qiwen, to Pudong to investigate at 4 p.m. yesterday. The district chief then ordered detectives Zhang Chunting, et al., to cooperate with the police to search the agency. On the spot, they seized a seal of the "Shanghai Finance Bureau Nanshi Pudong Superstition Scripture Donation Collection Branch," a letter of appointment for the director of the collection office, Zhong Yuanzhi, eleven blank appointment envelopes, which were found to be forged, and a collection book, a cash flow book, and a rent book. At that time, the director of the office, Zhong Yuan, was still out entertaining and did not recognize it as a cunning agency. The detectives took the witnesses, along with eleven collectors and Zhong's wife, Lin, to the Third District for processing. It was found that the main agency was located in Zhabei. District Chief Zhang immediately brought the case for preliminary interrogation. Zhong confessed that he was 36 years old, from Ningbo, and formerly served as the branch chief of the Lishui County Public Security Bureau. In February of this year, he was appointed by Zhang Youshi, the director of the Shanghai Finance Bureau Superstition Scripture Donation Collection Office, as the director of the Pudong Collection Branch, and obtained a letter of appointment. He then rented a house in Pudong to prepare for opening the branch. Recently, he was additionally appointed to handle Nanshi. He has been preparing for five months. Zhang has taken away 1,500 yuan in security deposits. All expenses during the preparation period totaled more than 1,000 yuan. The main agency is located at No. 144 Huzhou Road, Zhabei. Currently, the branch has recruited five or six people who donate 50 yuan each, all of whom have been registered. The collectors Yao Ningxing, Huang Jiachang, Chen Jinlian, Li Guowu, Chen Jichu, Lu Hai, Chen Jingru, Wang Rongqiang, Wang Zhibing, Zhu Daohui, and Luo Youcai successively confessed the same information. The district chief believes that these people may have been deceived and that the main agency is still in Zhabei, so he reported to the director by phone for investigation and arrest. Meanwhile, he sent all the witnesses to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Continued Interrogation of Wu Jiangguang, et al., Accused of Fraud

Yesterday's Debate Concluded

Order to Announce the Judgment on a Set Date

The well-known blind man Wu Jiangguang, et al., were sued by Kuomintang member Yu Qingyu in the Special District Local Court for the crime of using妖言惑衆 to defraud money. It has been interrogated twice and has been reported in the newspapers. It was interrogated again yesterday. Yu's wife, Chen, did not arrive. According to Yu, the various妖言惑衆 actions of the defendants not only harmed him personally, but also violated the Three Principles of the People, which is not allowed under the party's rule. Therefore, the personal loss is still light, but the responsibility for破坏主义 is difficult to forgive. Judge Feng Shide then asked whether the plaintiff's accusation that the defendants committed fraud was because the defendants improperly used exorcism and sold符咒. Yu said yes. Judge Feng instructed him, according to the confessions of the defendants Chai Caigao, et al., that the scriptures were not sold by them. Can you prove it? Yu said, then who sold the scriptures obtained by my wife? Chai should be ordered to confess clearly. Yu continued, during the previous court hearing, the defendant's lawyer, Ye Fukan, brought a fake Wu Jiangguang to court to pretend to be the real Wu Jiangguang and asked my wife to identify him. Although my wife mistakenly identified the fake as the real one at that time, this was not my wife's mistake. When my wife went to Wu's place, Wu was upstairs, and his disciple did a reading for her. My wife mistakenly thought this disciple was Wu himself. The fake Wu Jiangguang who came to court the other day was the disciple who did the reading in the past, so she still mistakenly identified him. When questioned about the various accusations made by Yu, Wu and the other five defendants consistently denied them. Then, after mutual arguments by the lawyers of both parties, Zhang Chongding and Ye Fukan, the court instructed both parties to withdraw and wait for the judgment to be announced on a set date.

The Jardine Matheson Ship that Had an Accident in Nanyang Has Arrived in Shanghai

The Shipowner Describes the Cause of the Accident

There Is a Novelist on Board

Traveling the World with His Wife

Obtaining Good Material at Sea

The North China Daily News reported that the refrigerated cargo ship De Li Cheng, managed by Jardine Matheson, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning after an accident in Nanyang and docked at the Pootung Blue Funnel Wharf. According to the shipowner, on the fifth of this month, the ship was sailing between Singapore and Hong Kong when it suddenly saw thick smoke rising from the ventilator of the third cargo hold in the early morning. He immediately ordered an inspection and found that the coal loaded in the hold was on fire. At that time, the hold contained more than 1,000 tons of English coal, which was shipped from England to the East, so the situation was extremely serious. He immediately gathered the crew and poured water into the hold from above, but it was ineffective for a long time. Therefore, a hole was drilled in the coal in the lower deck, leading to the fire, and a

Page 16

belt was inserted to pour water, which gradually extinguished the fire. During this time, the crew rescued day and night, very bravely. As for the cause of the accident, it was probably due to prolonged exposure to the hot sea, which caused a chemical reaction and spontaneous combustion, which could not be prevented by human power. When the ship arrived in Hong Kong and the coal was unloaded, it was found that a considerable amount had been burned to ashes and coke, which shows the intensity of the fire. The famous Australian novelist Colin and his wife were on board, traveling the world to collect materials, and also came to Shanghai. According to the shipowner, because Mr. and Mrs. Colin were greatly frightened, the fare was not collected. Colin was very fortunate to have obtained a good material for maritime life and hopes that there will be good works in the future to offer to the world.

The Disturbance During the Construction of Buildings at Jinan University

Misunderstanding Among Local Workers

Accountant Severely Injured by Chopping

Accident on the Way to the Hospital

Car Runs Over Pedestrian's Finger

A dormitory is being built at Zhenru Jinan University, which is contracted by Jiang Hengji Construction Factory. The factory employs Zhang Peixing, a 28-year-old accountant from Nanxiang. He is young, capable, and resourceful. He is usually deeply trusted by the factory owner, so he is entrusted with all matters, large and small. At that time, a large number of carpenters were hired, mostly from Nanxiang. Later, because the school authorities needed the buildings when the next semester started, they had to add dozens of workers locally to speed up the completion. They worked in peace for more than ten days. A few days ago, the local carpenters reported to the accountant Zhang Peixing that the quality of the wood was uneven and unsuitable for work, and they wanted to add better wood. Zhang replied that the building was about to be completed. Could they use it temporarily? If it was absolutely unusable, please suspend work temporarily, and after reporting to the factory owner, wait for the good materials to be transported before starting work again. When the workers heard this, they misunderstood that he was arrogant and deliberately making things difficult for the local people. In the afternoon, they gathered all the local carpenters and held a meeting in a nearby teahouse. As a result, they believed that it was an insult to the local workers and decided to strike. At more than 7 p.m. that night, a group of workers gathered at the accountant's office to reason with Zhang Peixing. They destroyed the accountant's office when a word was said amiss. Fortunately, Peixing was rescued by others to avoid the disaster. Wait for the factory owner to come and solve the problem again. Unexpectedly, at about 12 noon yesterday, the Nanxiang workers and Zhang Peixing were having lunch when dozens of local people arrived with weapons such as axes and iron bars. Without asking the reason, they suddenly took action. The Nanxiang workers fled because they had no weapons. Peixing was chopped on his two arms, shoulder bones, and left foot with an axe, and a Nanxiang worker, Qiang Liansheng, was chopped on his arm with an axe, about three or four inches deep. Blood flowed non-stop, and the injury was serious. The murderers then dispersed. They immediately called the Linji car company near Si Malu Qinghefang and ordered the driver to drive car No. 17577 to the destination, carrying the two injured people in the car to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, when the car passed the old garbage bridge, because the speed was too high, the rickshaw driver Xia Er (50 years old) from Jiangbei was knocked to the ground and his fingers were crushed. He was arrested by post No. 2205 and transported to Baolong Hospital for treatment.

Director Yan of the Public Security Bureau Supervised the Oath-Taking on the Spot

believed that there were many roads built across the border, and defense was especially important, and that Daxi Road was the most important. New Organization in China's Radio Industry

Named China United Radio Company

Domestic manufacturers of radio equipment include the Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant of the Construction Committee, the Zhonghua Sanji Rui Electric Company, the Dahua Scientific Instrument Company, and the Hongkang Electric Material Store. It is found that almost all radio equipment erected in Shanghai is supervised and manufactured by the above four manufacturers. Recently, in order to develop and promote China's radio business, the four manufacturers have concentrated their strength, expanded their scope, and jointly organized the "China United Radio Company" at No. 3, Museum Road, Shanghai. Ding Zuocheng, Wang Zhenxiang, Zhu Qiqing, Wu Weiyue, Yu Ruxin, Tao Jun, Zhang Tingjin, Yan Renguang, and others carefully planned and divided into a board of directors and an engineering department to respectively assume the company's progress matters. Zhu Qiqing was appointed as the chairman of the first board of directors, and Wu Weiyue was appointed as the chairman of the first engineering department. The above gentlemen are all radio experts and occupy a very important position in the radio industry. Their reputation is well-known and admired by the Chinese people. Now they are jointly organizing a company to preside over everything. From now on, the company can undertake all the latest radio equipment. It is predicted that in the future, the United Company will make a great contribution to the country and society.

Cholera Prevention Plan in Luhang District

Cholera was prevalent in Luhang District, Pudong, last year. According to the investigation by the Public Security Bureau, in May of the 18th year of the Republic of China, 11 men and 3 women died. In June, 103 men and 56 women died. In July, 126 men and 92 women died. In the above three months, a total of 391 people died, and the local loss can be said to be huge. Therefore, Zhang Qiwen, a municipal commissioner of the district, and Qu Shaoji, a citizen, visited Director Hu of the Health Bureau the day before yesterday (17th) to discuss the establishment of a temporary epidemic prevention hospital. Director Hu said that the municipal treasury was in financial difficulty, and it was difficult to run an epidemic prevention hospital. For fundamental prevention, citizens could be persuaded to inject epidemic prevention needles. Based on the current situation this year, it is quite effective. Committee Member Zhang, et al., now plan to invite each圖董 to gather to discuss the method of persuading injection, and then ask the Health Bureau to send a doctor to inject.

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Reorganizes Shanghai South Public Bus Stops

The stops of the first, second, and third routes of the Shanghai South public buses are mostly located close to the tram stops where they run parallel to the tracks of Huashang trams. As a result, when the two types of vehicles arrive at the station at the same time, other vehicles are blocked. In view of this, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities sent personnel to survey and determine the locations where the public buses should be moved, and then re-examined and agreed with the Engineering Bureau. It was immediately listed and ordered the company to follow the relocation in order to improve the situation. It is now known that the company has moved all the stations along the tram tracks in accordance with the list.

Fortunately, No One Was Injured

The houses in Jiqingli, Yokohamabashi, North Sichuan Road, collapsed at 2:30 p.m. yesterday (18th) with a loud crash. Six houses in the third alley collapsed. Fortunately, no one was injured. Yu Xia Agrees to Divorce with 100 Yuan

Yu Qiugan, the owner of the Xintai Fresh Meat Shop at Xingjia Benmu Bridge, Zhabei, is 22 years old and is from Chuansha, Pudong. Because his wife, Yu Xia (i.e., Xia Muying), ran away repeatedly, it was difficult to grow old together. He hired lawyer Yan Dajue to file a lawsuit for divorce in the local court. His words were slightly said that on the 16th day of the first month of the 11th year of the Republic of China, his parents were in charge and hired Xia Xidu's daughter Muying as his wife, but she was naturally bad and it was difficult to harmonize the qin and se. She ran away from her husband and escaped three times. The first time was in July of the twelfth year, and she ran away for about a week. Later, the original matchmaker sent her back. In August of the thirteenth year, she ran away for the second time, taking things with her and disappearing without a trace. It was more than a year before she was found by trying to find her in September of the following year (fourteenth year). There were often conflicts between the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law. On May 30 of this year's national calendar, she ran away for the third time. At that time, she had requested the Public Security Bureau and various police stations to investigate and arrest her, but she could not find her after repeated searches. She had no choice but to publish a notice on June 1 to break away from the relationship between husband and wife. Although she has been found back, she still thinks of escaping in the gap. In this situation, it is difficult to grow old together. The only thing is to divorce her. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Jinjian specially opened the fourth court to conduct a trial. According to the plaintiff Yu Qiuquan's confession of the previous situation, he requested permission to divorce. (Question) What reasons are you basing on? (Answer) She often runs away, regardless of family affairs. (Question) Who is the matchmaker? (Answer) Du Quanyuan, and there is a Yu who died. (Question) Have you always been harmonious? (Answer) She is lazy and unwilling to work. She ran away three times in total. After publishing the notice to break away this time, her family sent her back a week later. Next, the defendant Xia Muying provided a confession, age 23. (Question) Where did you go? (Answer) At my mother's house. (Question) Have you been anywhere else? (Answer) No. (Question) How long did you live in your mother's house this time? (Answer) Half a month, because he beat me, so I ran back to my mother's house. (Question) Your husband now wants a divorce, what do you think? (Answer) I don't have any intentions, he doesn't want me, there is no way. (Question) How is it going? (Answer) His heart is unwilling, and my heart is also unwilling. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer said that the defendant had said outside that she was willing to divorce. The questioning official asked the defendant again and again, and her attitude finally stated that divorce was possible, but she needed 500 yuan for living expenses. When asked about the plaintiff, he only allowed to pay 10-20 yuan. The intermediary official repeatedly advised both parties. As a result, the plaintiff paid the defendant 100 yuan, and both parties expressed their willingness. Therefore, a settlement was reached and they divorced each other. The questioning official wrote out the settlement record and ordered both parties to sign and leave the court.

Former Honorary Leader of the Sports Advancement Association

Shen Siliang Returned to China Yesterday

A Large Crowd Welcomed Him at the Dock

He Described the State of American Sports

Hoping Our Country Will Promote It Universally

In Addition to Serving as Vice President of Shanghai University

He Will Still Strive to Promote Sports

Investigating Educational Administration: Mr. Shen Siliang, Acting Vice President of Shanghai University and former honorary leader of the All-China Sports Advancement Association, traveled to the United States with his wife and children last July. In addition to investigating educational administration and sports, he attended Columbia University to study education under Dr. Dewey and obtained a Master of Education degree this summer. Mr. Shen formerly specialized in sports at Springfield College in the United States. This time, revisiting old haunts, many friends came to meet him, and he did not feel lonely in a foreign land.

Refereeing Ball Games in the U.S.: While in the United States, he was highly regarded by the country's sports circles. He was invited to serve as a referee for major soccer games three times and a basketball game once. It is rare for a Chinese person to serve as a referee in the United States.

Relatives and Friends Welcomed Him at the Dock: Mr. Shen returned to China yesterday with his wife and children on the Chichibu Maru, arriving at the Wharf at 4 p.m. More than a hundred people from Shanghai's sports circles and his relatives and friends, including Shen Sixin, Hao Boyang, Wu Bangwei, Zhao Xiuhong, Xu Zhendong, Ma Chonggan, Zhang Shilin, Huang Weilian, Sun Daosheng, and Li Baojun, went to the dock to welcome him.

[Image Caption: Mr. Shen Siliang, his wife, and daughter arriving in Shanghai yesterday (photographed by Ye Changlie)]

Talking to the Reporter: After the greetings, Mr. Shen shared with the reporter his observations on the state of sports in the United States. He said that professional competitions are common in the United States, and English football is also very popular. The development of sports in the United States is due to its universal promotion, not just focusing on a few items. People in the U.S. did not pay much attention to the Far Eastern Games, so few people knew about it. Regarding his views on developing sports in China, he believes that one must start from the basics and not just seek temporary radicalism, which would not help in practice. He also hopes that the directors of the Sports Advancement Association will quickly plan for a permanent location for the association and, more importantly, quickly determine a plan for universal promotion, dividing the work and cooperating to advance in all regions. In three to five years, Chinese sports will have a new look, he said. As for Mr. Shen's return to China, he will still serve as the vice president of Shanghai University and will do his best to promote sports. Whether he can serve in the Sports Advancement Association is still uncertain.

Shanghai University Welcomes Him Tonight: Mr. Shen returned to Shanghai University by car at six o'clock in the evening. The faculty and staff will hold a welcome party at the school at 6:30 tonight.

Zhu Kuan, Sun Daosheng, and Lu Dangbai Win

After the All-Shanghai Handball Championship, organized by the YMCA, concluded last week, the champions and runners-up of Groups A, B, and C, as well as famous players such as Zhu Kuan, initiated an invitational tournament, which was held at the YMCA handball court at 5:30 p.m. yesterday. The results of yesterday's competition are described below:

Zhu Kuan Engages in Fierce Battle with Hong Yukui: Zhu Kuan is a famous player in the handball world, and his exquisite skills need no further elaboration. Hong Yukui is the champion of Group A, young and strong, and can be called a rising star, but his experience is slightly inferior. In the confrontation between the two, Zhu Kuan showed off his skills and repeatedly made outstanding contributions, once winning by a large margin of 16-0. Seeing the unfavorable situation, Yukui quickly caught up and scored many points in a row. However, the momentum had already become a prairie fire and was difficult to reverse. As a result, Zhu Kuan won the first game 21-9. From the second game onwards, Yukui's momentum suddenly increased, and Zhu Kuan suddenly became weak. As a result, Yukui won 21-8. The strengths of both sides were equal, and a third game should have been played to determine the winner. Later, they agreed to abandon the unplayed game.

Sun Daosheng Defeats Hong Rulin: Sun Daosheng is the runner-up of Group A, and his strength and experience are very sufficient. Hong Rulin is the champion of Group B. The competition between the two sides was quite fierce. Daosheng used both his left and right hands, doing whatever he wanted, making Hong Rulin lose sight of one thing while attending to another and exhausted. As a result, Mr. Sun won two consecutive games 21-9, 21-9.

Lu Aibai Defeats Cheng Zhenhua: Lu is the runner-up of Group B, and Cheng is the champion of Group C. In the confrontation, it was difficult to distinguish the winner. In the first game, Lu won 21-13. From the second game onwards, Cheng seemed to be doing well, and the score exceeded several times, but Lu was unwilling to show weakness and worked hard, and the score jumped to the lead. Cheng followed closely behind, reaching 18-18. Lu continued his efforts and finally won again with 21-18.

The referee for the competition was Gu Yongzhao, and the recorder was Ling Xitao.
