Free Talk

Talking About the Capital in the Scorching Heat: Zhang Yan

Convenient Pavilions for Pedestrians: Zhongshan Road in the capital is a necessary thoroughfare for entering and leaving the city. The traffic is like clouds, and the pedestrians are like weaving. Even Nanjing Road in Shanghai is not as crowded. The current authorities, for the convenience of pedestrians relieving themselves, have specially built four urinals, located in sections along Zhongshan Road. The pavilions are about nine feet high, with flying eaves at the corners, painted in red. They are protected by wooden skirts, shaped like octagons, about three feet shorter than the pavilions, painted in dark green. Viewed from afar, the red and green complement each other, and they are exquisite and unique. People find them convenient, so everyone calls them "Convenient Pavilions."

Many Cold Drink Shops: The capital is hot, even more so than in previous years. In the area of Confucius Temple and Sanshanfu East Street in the south of the city, and Zhongshan Road and Guofu Street in the center of the city, and the area north of the city, many cold drink shops (selling ice cream and soda, etc.) have sprung up. Every few steps, you can see white flags with red characters and soft signboards fluttering in the wind. Some have specially opened elegant rooms, with white cloths covering the tables, flowers in vases, and arranged seats. Others are simple and crude, placing two dining tables in the shop, covered with white cloths, and placing three or four pots of wintergreen grass flowers in front of the door to attract customers and do good business.

Lively Mochou Lake: Mochou Lake is located outside Shuixi Gate in the capital. The lake site covers a large area and has beautiful scenery, making it the best place to escape the summer heat. At the moment, the lotus flowers in the lake are in full bloom. Countless men and women from the city come here to enjoy the cool breeze and admire the lotus flowers. The fragrance of the flowers and the shadows of their hair reflect in the heart of the lake, which is very pleasant. The fragrant lotus roots produced in the lake are the most famous. The lotus roots are crisp and fat, with fine and tender flesh, as white as ice and snow. Although the taste is not as sweet as the lotus roots of West Lake, it is juicy and fragrant, surpassing those of West Lake.

Buses Start Running, Streetcars Stop Running for a Long Time: The long-awaited buses officially started running on the 11th. There are more than 20 passenger cars. The first route runs from Xiaguan to Huangpu Road, divided into ten stations. Each stop costs 12 copper coins. A bus runs every ten minutes. The entire route takes about 40 minutes. As for the rickshaws pulled by coolies, due to the excessive heat, their flesh and blood bodies cannot withstand the scorching sun, so streetcars have been scarce for days. Even if there are any, the prices are raised because of this. Passengers do not even have time to haggle over the price, which shows that there are too few streetcars.

A Formula for Killing Bedbugs: Tao Zaidong

A comrade of this publication, seeing the bedbug-killing formula recorded by me, thought it was magical and wonderful. He telephoned me and asked me to announce the formula for imitation. I had said before that I had no right to refuse. Now I will announce this formula, but I must first announce the person who taught me this formula. That person is a stunningly beautiful woman, named Bian Zizhi, whose former self was one of the flower fairies, the Michelia alba fairy. She has both talent and beauty, and her personality is humorous. I met her in my childhood in "Romance of the Flowers in the Mirror," and she told me this formula. The formula is very simple, and I recommend imitating it and adding one or two ingredients. I must say this first because it is a scholar's virtue not to betray the teacher or steal the credit. The formula is recorded as follows:

Zizhi Fairy Teaches Tao Ling's Wonderful Formula for Killing Bedbugs:

Clean (sufficient weight) - Fingers

(Wash two) - Diligent Catch (one ingredient)

Words of Wisdom: Qiushui

The longer young people live in this world, the more they despise society, despise friends, and even despise themselves. Although a man hands the key to his heart to a woman and marries her, he never wants his heart to be opened once and then closed again.

Women's hearts can be said to be the most gentle. But when she hears the news that her old flame is marrying someone else and feels dissatisfied, she cannot control a slight sense of self-satisfaction and pleasure in her heart.

In the eyes of some wives, many men are like old-fashioned jewelry: it's a pity to throw them away, but they are useless to keep. They don't know how to arrange him. Perhaps she occasionally feels like putting him on, but this is not because of his valuable worth, but just a matter of emotion.

Men have invented substitutes for coal, substitutes for food, substitutes for diamonds, and even substitutes for youth. But they have not invented substitutes for women, substitutes for can openers, and substitutes for pants.

Freedom is sweeter than coffee for women, but the moment of a man's first kiss is sweeter than freedom and coffee.

Random Notes on a Trip to Hangzhou (Part 1): Huang Jiping

The Hangzhou YMCA recently formed a Journalism Research Society. Its purpose is to arouse young people's interest in studying journalism and to provide a platform for those in the journalism field to exchange knowledge. Recently, the society specially invited senior journalist Ge Gongzhen to give a lecture. I also went with him. First, we exchanged letters and decided to depart by night train one day and return on the 5th. The intention of this trip was to observe the social situation of Hangzhou in addition to sightseeing. Unfortunately, the summer heat was overwhelming and the time was short, so I did not gain much. I write this down in a haphazard manner, just to fill a space.

The express train was delayed that night and only left the North Station at 6:20. I leaned against the window and looked out idly. The area north of Shanghai is densely packed with factories, which is probably the most prosperous industrial area of Shanghai. Looking back to the west, there were vegetable gardens, ridges, bamboo fences, and thatched huts. Separated by a single track, the material disparity was almost like being in a different world. Leaving Longhua, the golden crow set in the west, and the scenery outside the window could no longer be distinguished. Sitting upright in the carriage, Mr. Ge recounted his experiences of traveling around the world the year before. The prosperity of the cities and the wild scenery of the villages were quite interesting. He also showed the films of the news industry in various countries that he had brought with him, explaining them to me one by one. I learned about the large newspaper offices and news agencies of Britain, America, France, Germany, Italy, and Japan. Seeing the spaciousness of their buildings, the completeness of their organizations, the intensity of their work, and the breadth of their business, one could not help but admire them. Each newspaper office spared no expense in using science to strive for perfection, wanting the news to be accurate. They hired experts to conduct interviews and used telephoto photography to verify the information, seeking to deliver the news quickly. They had their own trains, airplanes, and transport ships to deliver the news across the country in three to four hours, aiming to provide convenience. They set up their own factories to manufacture machinery, paper, ink. In addition to daily newspapers, they also published morning editions, noon editions, evening editions, and night editions. Events of the day were recorded in the newspapers of the same day. I realized that modern newspapers have reached the extreme of capitalization, specialization, and scientification, beyond what we can imagine. They have already realized what we can't achieve. Other examples include the communication agencies that manipulate public opinion, such as Reuters in Britain, Associated Press in the United States, Continental Telegraph Company in Germany, Agence Havas in France, and Rengo News Agency in Japan. They sent personnel to various capitals to organize a communication network. Whenever something happened, there was a report. They manipulated the right and wrong, and small countries suffered greatly. Our country's diplomatic failures over the years have mostly been affected by their counter-propaganda... I

Listened to his words with a sense of awe. Mr. and Mrs. American Mingside, who were sitting in the same seat with me, understood Chinese and were delighted to hear us talking so enthusiastically. I exchanged pleasantries with them. They said they had been traveling in Hangzhou for 20 years and were very familiar with the local customs. We talked about the national customs of China and the United States and laughed together. We arrived in Hangzhou at 11 o'clock, where newspaper colleagues and close friends had been waiting for a long time.

Record of the Autumn Pavilion: Jing Mengdie

The reason for the existence of the Autumn Pavilion in the Mei Garden is due to the autumn of the Bingyin year and completed in the Wuwu year. It is called Autumn Red to record the fact. The one who named it was the owner, but it was the creation of nature. Previously, there was a clump of peonies in front of the pavilion. That year, in the ninth autumn, when the chrysanthemums were about to bloom, the thousands of chrysanthemums in the garden were still in bud, as if waiting for something. One day, the owner was talking with me in the mansion when the gardener suddenly reported that the peony was blooming. Alas, Tao Yuanming's three paths actually learned from peach trees. The Yao and Wei families were replaced by the Li family, which is indeed a unique case. The owner was delighted to hear this and immediately invited me to go and see it with him. Upon arrival, I saw a pot specially placed on the table, with deep purple flowers and green leaves supporting it, truly resembling the spring colors.

Glimpses of a Trip to the East (12): Qian Hua

Regarding equipment, the Mainichi Shimbun has one American-made high-speed photogravure printing press that can print 120,000 copies per hour, and another high-speed machine that can print 72,000 copies per hour, 12 presses, 14 type-casting machines, seven stereotype machines, six photoengraving machines, one telephoto photogravure machine, and seven aircrafts, over one hundred carrier pigeons. There are 685 employees and 1,442 workers. The Asahi Shimbun is even more exquisite and complete, with 17 ultra-high-speed Asahi-style rotary presses that can print 130,000 copies per hour, one German-made four-color printing rotary press, two American-made rotary presses, nine flatbed printing presses, one telephoto photogravure machine, and 16 aircrafts. The number of employees and workers is about the same as the Mainichi Shimbun. There are 250 carrier pigeons. The news for both newspapers is provided by the employees themselves. They rarely use news from communication agencies such as the Electricity News and Reuters. They use long-distance telephone and aircraft communication throughout the country. Long-distance photos are transmitted by telephoto machines. They set up communication bureaus in various places, each headed by an employee. The same is true overseas. All major cities around the world have correspondents stationed there. The communication network can be said to be tight. Each newspaper earns hundreds of thousands of dollars of profit each year, which is used for public reserve funds, shareholder and employee dividends, employee pensions, and a part is used for the development of social public services. For example, last year, the Osaka Mainichi East Asia Investigation Committee was established, and Count Kiyoura Keigo, Count Uchida Kosai, and Baron Hayashi Gonsuke and ten other people were hired as consultants. The Committee hosted a health promotion sports meet, set up free clinics, and held the 11th National Junior High School Soccer Tournament, the 5th National Women's Sports Games, the 8th National Tennis Player Competition, and provided subsidies for various charitable causes. According to their claims, the consumption of these subsidiary businesses in the past five years has reached 2 million yen. The Asahi Shimbun's subsidiary businesses have been most successful in developing aviation and sports. Its aviation and sports departments are full of talent and were once extremely prosperous. The Asahi Sports Monthly, hosted by the sports department, is particularly praised. Its sales cover the entire country. The aviation department has 16 aircrafts. In January of the Taisho 12th year (1923), Asahi sponsored the start of regular air service between Tokyo and Osaka. On August 17 of the Showa 3rd year (1928), it began to transport passengers and mail, and its business was extremely developed, opening a new era in the Japanese aviation industry. Last April 1, the business was taken over by Japan Air Transport Co., Ltd. Over the years, Asahi lost 732,391 yen. In addition, Asahi bore 408,972 yen for the long-distance flight to Europe. Last year, it held the International Water Sports Competition and the East-West Confrontation Track and Field Sports Meet. Also last year, for the 50th anniversary of Asahi, various celebrations were extremely prosperous, and it proposed 500,000 yen in subsidies for various social undertakings and 1 million yen to be distributed as rewards to all employees. The Asahi Shimbun used the power of aviation to make its news particularly outstanding. It was fast and accurate, which other newspapers could not match. For example, three years ago, when Zhang Zuolin was bombed in Huanggu Tun, Asahi quickly sent five aircrafts to collect news. The next morning, the photos and news were dazzling, and people are still praising them. Other companies, such as the Osaka Jiji Shinpo, also had slight surpluses each year, but they were not as good as Asahi and Mainichi.

That is also the reason. Why would there be red in the deep autumn? Perhaps the god of spring loves famous gardens, so he made an uninvited visit. This is enough to break the record of the Luoyang flower catalog. When the viewers became crowded, they all said that peony belongs to wealthy flowers, competing to congratulate the owner for his late success. I said that wealth is not very important to the owner. However, to see the spring glory again in the bleak autumn season is like a person being old but not aging. This is a sign of longevity and is enough to praise the owner. The owner thought it was true, so he ordered a photograph to record the event. I wrote a poem titled: "It is not Henan or Luoyang; The flower king is seen in the season of yellow flowers; He especially uses the national color to intoxicate the autumn color; Who says that the heavenly fragrance occupies the late fragrance? The old scene teaches people to boast of wealth; The delicate appearance is also resistant to wind and frost; Long spring foreshadows the blessing of the god of spring; A tree of wonderful flowers reports auspiciousness."

The pavilion is located to the west of the Songbin Hall, so it has no name. The owner recently told me that he would personally write the three characters "Autumn Red Pavilion" to adorn it. Mr. Sun Songtuo also made a couplet for it: "Brew a small spring in September, famous flowers bloom in autumn; Collect a pavilion in ten thousand acres, the beautiful scenery is natural." I also used the Phoenix-crown style to embed the two characters "Autumn Red" into a couplet: "Autumn season sees spring glory; the scenery of September resides with the God of Spring; Red sincerity maintains the national plan; the famous traces of Five Lakes continue Zhu Gong." This pavilion is located near the Five Lakes, facing the Taozhu Pavilion on Yuanzhu Island from afar. The owner has always attached importance to education in addition to running real estate. He always speaks of producing and teaching. He has long admired the personality of Fan Shaobo.

Brief News: Changsha Quan Juanzhi, an old man known for his calligraphy, has long been admired at home and abroad. Recently, at the request of the Weiran Calligraphy and Painting Society, he set a rate to meet the desires of those who love the old man's ink treasures. Inquiries can be sent to No. 1324, Intersection of Aiwenyi Road and Hede Road.

Lin Gui Kuang Youhan, painted ancient style landscape fans at the request of fellow students of Xilu, following the old practice of reducing the price in the summer for two months. Inquiries about the reduced price can be sent to Kuang Xiaosong, 3rd floor, Shenbao.

Heartfelt Warmth (336) by Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Twelve: Farewell Banquet, Parting Feast, Holding Flowers to Capture a Beautiful Image; Famous Garden Gathering, Tea Competition to Behold Elegant Charms

Zuo Shichen said, "I'm hungry. Let's find a place to have supper. After supper, we'll go to other places." Long Ziyun said, "There's Japanese cuisine here. It's said that the wife of the head of Mitsui & Co. is in charge there. Japanese people, regarding that kind of voluntary garden party, many noble ladies participate. Let's go and have a look." Zuo Shichen said, "I can't speak Japanese; it's no fun." Long Ziyun said, "I can manage a few simple sentences. Fortunately, Japan and we share the same writing system. Where language fails, we can still communicate with writing. Just use a pencil and paper and write it for them. Besides, we haven't had Japanese food in a long time. Why not try it today?" Zuo Shichen agreed. The two walked into the Japanese restaurant. Sure enough, there were several Japanese beauties dressed in finery who came to greet them. They were very respectful to the guests. Fortunately, they didn't recognize who they were. The menu was printed, a combination of Chinese and Japanese. Even if there was no Chinese, they could still understand the Japanese. They also ordered a bottle of Taiyo Beer. They saw a young girl carrying a bottle of wine and two glasses on a purple lacquered tray, placing them on the table. She bowed deeply. Long and Zuo saw that she was a student, not a servant. They didn't know whose daughter she was and could only return her bow. However, they were somewhat burdened afterward. Every time she brought a dish, she would bow. They had to return the bow at least once. After finishing this Japanese meal, they didn't know how many bows they had made or how many courtesies they had returned. Zuo Shichen smiled and said to Long Ziyun, "Well, this overly courteous banquet, no matter how grand, didn't have every dish require a bow. Eating this Japanese food is too uneconomical." Long Ziyun said, "That's not it. You have to know that they are used to sitting on the floor. Also, they consider themselves versed in etiquette. When sitting on the floor, everyone is kneeling. Even bowing to you only requires placing both hands on the ground and leaning forward. Moreover, women are subordinate to men. For example, when they have guests at home, when his wife serves wine and food, she even kowtows every time. The woman considers it a matter of course, while the husband simply ignores her. Now, they are not sitting on the floor here, so they deliberately kowtow to make a bow. In reality, they are accustomed to it. Without doing so, they cannot be considered versed in etiquette." After finishing the Japanese food, Long Ziyun paid the bill and they came out. It was already past eight o'clock, and the number of visitors was gradually increasing. Over there was a tea tasting area. It was originally a vegetable garden. Now, beside the eastern corner, there was a bamboo grove with dozens of seats. It was said that the owner of Wei Garden set it up himself.

Financial Silver Bar Stability

There was no strong change. Yesterday, the 28th, the price of silver bars showed some potential, but there was no strong change. In the morning session, there was a fluctuation of five taels. In the afternoon session, there was still a review of four taels. As for foreign exchange, it was still firm. Banks had varying inflows and outflows. The demand from various firms in the market was quite different. Hengxing, Wanxing, Shunli, etc., all had deposits, while Yuanmao, Yongda, Decheng, Fuxing, Yong, etc., all sold out. People were uneasy and lacked intention. The market opened lower in the morning, probably because the rebound in the silver market influenced the subsequent trend towards stability. Only a few lots briefly reached 605 taels, but due to the frequent decline in spot prices, they turned weak again, suddenly falling to the 600 tael mark. Later, Hengxing, Zhifeng, Yong, Yuanmao, Yong, etc., still made purchases, while Yuansheng, Yuancheng, Yongda, Decheng, etc., sold. The market situation returned to kindness, with only one or two tael fluctuations. Exchange rates were slightly better, later fluctuating between 603 taels. Yesterday, London silver bars rose by three-sixteenths, forward added one-eighth, and silver prices rose by one-quarter.

Before noon closing, there was a slight downward trend. The initial price of gold for September was 601 taels and 9 mace, a decrease of 1 tael and 4 mace. Later, buyers became active, gradually increasing by two taels and several qian, to 604 taels and a half. As for foreign exchange, it did not loosen. In August, British gold interbank trading was six pence one eight seven five. Although the Bank of England announced the listing price, it did not move. Internally, it stabilized, but Hengxing, etc., slightly released notes, so it returned to 3 taels and 3 qian, then saw 4 taels. After ten o'clock, it retreated to 2 taels 6 or 7 qian, but various exchanges were still able to stand firm and did not loosen. September British gold Sino-French and Hua-Belgian interbank trading was six pence two five, and Hengxing bought in again, so it rose to 604 taels 8 qian. Later, Fuxing, Yong, Yuanmao, Yong, Zhifeng, Yong, etc., all sold because the spot market was quite weak. The market situation turned firm, and then added one or two taels, but soon fell by three taels, suddenly breaking the 600 tael mark, only calculated at 99 taels and 7 qian. After 11:30, it still jumped out of the gate, closing at 600 taels and 0.05 qian at noon.

Suddenly, Xinhang and others sold off, losing 1 tael 4 or 5 qian. At 2:30, it was 600 taels 0.02 qian. After entering, McCallum bought in, and Xia Yong and others purchased, so it increased by two or three taels, to 1:00 being 603 taels 1 qian. Linghu and others took the opportunity to sell, retreating 1 tael, calculated as 1 tael 8 or 9 qian. After 3:30, it gradually rose. Suddenly, it was heard that a certain bank seemed to have the intention of buying spot goods. For a time, the atmosphere in the market was good, adding more than two taels. At 4:00, it was calculated as 604 taels 2 qian, but rumors were 3 taels 2 qian, still falling by 1 qian compared to the day before. Guangdong merchants replenished 2,000 bars. Although the transactions of various firms were not deserted, the demands were different. Arts and Literature

The Poetry of Black People by Yang Changxi

The system of black slavery in America has undergone a long history. They turned and tossed in the life of slaves, working hard day and night for the deep authority of their masters. They felt that white people were specially created by God to oppress them, and they believed that their suffering was driven by fate. Therefore, in their long history, there was no resistance or accusation. However, since Lincoln formally liberated the black slaves, in the past fifty or sixty years, black people have gradually gained status economically, socially, and professionally. Apart from the stable lives of those who have acquired American citizenship, the majority of black people still live in a disguised form of slavery, with the difference that the abuse is relatively less.

Therefore, the liberated black people have gained educational opportunities. The various inequalities between ethnic groups felt by intellectuals are reflected in literature.

In our complete review of American black poetry, we can discover the following types of thinking:

(1) Forgetting the suffering they endure in reality, believing that they will never find comfort and happiness in this world, and taking conversion to God as their only consolation. They do not think of relieving the pain of reality, but only want to die early, only want "to go to heaven, sit on the throne of angels, eat the treasures of the angels... to be comfortable and happy, I and my God, can do whatever we want." Only wanting "the sweet and lovely car to sway and lower, it is coming to take me home... By my ability I have carefully investigated Canaan (GORDAND), behind me there is a team of angels, they are coming to take me home." In this kind of poetry, the former is the sad groan of black people in slave life who yearn for freedom, completely wanting to escape the oppression and suffering of the world. The latter is a hymn dreaming of Canaan, comparing themselves to the Israelite refugees who suffered in ancient Egypt, dreaming that God has chosen the fertile Canaan for them black slaves as the residence of the chosen people. However, earthly suffering is not lessened by the praise of God. Only in the religious anesthetic that is used by white people can it reduce their hatred of white people and eliminate their national consciousness. Not only can the dreamed-of Canaan not become the kingdom of the chosen people,

but even their motherland, Africa, has no place for them.

(2) The attitude of contentment. They praise the forests and thickets under the scorching heat of Africa, recall the situation in their hometown when they were young, sing the beauty of black girls, chant the material civilization of the United States, and praise the scenery of nature. This is because they have gone from being slaves to having the opportunity to receive higher education, and with a relatively better social status, they can safely chant everything without using literature as a signal to awaken national consciousness. Furthermore, perhaps some of them have already become American citizens and are singing, "I am the darker brother, when friends come to treat them, they call me to eat in the kitchen, but I smile, eat well, and grow strong... Tomorrow when friends come to treat them, I can sit at the table, and no one dares to say to me, go to the kitchen to eat... They can see how beautiful I am, how ashamed they are... Ah, I am also an American." They throw their whole body and mind into the kingdom of the white people.

(3) The performance of loyal slaves. Because they have lost their national identity after being immersed and molded for many years, they do not understand what the difference between white people and black people is, nor do they understand whether their masters' lives are slavery, and they are very loyal to their work. Therefore, in all the poems of black people, the most loved by workers are the more than ten poems describing John Henry (JOHN HENRY), which profoundly depict how black people have simply become loyal slaves after more than a hundred years of molding. Although some poems believe that John Henry is a railroad worker, and some believe that they are loyal steel workers, John Henry is loyal to his profession and decides to work day and night, deciding to die holding a hammer is common. Therefore, in a poem most loved by workers, Henry only says, "One person is always one person, I will always work with everyone, I will definitely die holding a hammer." He even said to his supervisor, "A person is finally a person, I will work day and night, and decide to die holding a hammer." But later, when he went up the mountain to strike down the steam drilling rig, because the stone was too high and his strength was too small, he finally died when he put down the hammer. In another poem, the last words Henry said to his son before his death were that he hoped he would not do other things, but still be a steel worker like his father who had sacrificed his life. In this kind of poetry, it fully represents the loyal slave nature of a part of black people, and hopes that his son will inherit his career. This type of worker, John Henry, is praised and expected by white people.

However, these three kinds of performances are gradually overcome by the trend of the times. Because the oppressed and small nations in the world all want to break free from the shackles and run to a state of freedom and independence, the national awakening presented in recent black literature, especially in poetry, is more acute.

In the great disparity between the lives of masters and slaves, they have already felt that "the wife lives in a high-rise building, the nanny lives in the backyard, the wife holds a white hand to play, the nanny works hard all the time... the masters always ride horses, the black slaves work around him all the time, the masters sleep during the day, the black slaves dig underground" the suffering and happiness is too far apart. Moreover, the black slaves who hold hoes in the hot sun all day long to strongly pick seabird droppings for the masters as fertilizer, describe "white people wearing starched shirts sitting in the shade, God has given birth to the laziest people." And the conversion to God has lost faith, and the black people who have been reduced to the status of slaves have reached the position of national self-consciousness. Therefore, they sing, "Hey, I am black, but I am also black and lovable, I am as dark as the son of night, as dark as the deep cave, I am a tender branch belonging to a slave race, he cooperated to build a strong country, then you and I can get equal treatment in the world, courageous and strong like those people on the turbulent waves, holding up a banner high, her fluttering overthrows all opposition." It is a deep statement that the need to build an independent country is a major problem that black people feel today. Therefore, the American critic V. F. CALVERTON believes in his introduction to "The Anthology of American Black Literature" that "the starting point of black literature is national, and it is created for the national self-consciousness, singing for the national suffering, not for art for art's sake, and the rise of black literature will achieve the rise of the entire nation in the future due to the growth of literature," which can further confirm that black people must focus on national freedom and liberation for the problem of the future. Therefore, I will first talk about the poems that can fully express the black people's self-consciousness. Let me make another review of the performance of national consciousness in the novel later.

Literary Anecdotes

Celebration of Pinero's Seventy-First Birthday

Pinero is a great modern British playwright. He is praised by the modern critic William Archer as "a thoughtful and fair writer." His plays always tell the story of "a woman with a past history." He and Shaw, Carpenter, Wilde, and Wells (the great historian) were all dangerous figures at the time.

On May 9th, his seventy-first birthday, Mr. Hamilton specially wrote a book, "Pinero's Plays and His Actors," as a celebration. This book is the best material in the history of drama in the past fifty years. There are also many photos of (May June).

Page 23

The Story of World Literature (180) Written by John Macy of the United States, Translated by Hu Zhongchi

Chapter 47 American Novels

On the side of a mountain in New Hampshire, high up there is a cluster of rocks that form a huge human face, which is one of the natural wonders of the world and a sight known to all travelers. Hawthorne made "The Old Man of the Mountain" particularly his own. He imagined what kind of influence this would have on sensitive children growing up in its shadow. Therefore, in "The Great Stone Face," he thought of it as a symbol, an inspiration. He transformed the rock into a poetic sermon. Before Hawthorne wrote, New England was not known as "The Land of Fairies," but after he wrote, Romance adopted that place as one of its permanent residences.

Cooper and Irving and Hawthorne saw their works popular during their lifetime, and enjoyed as much practical prosperity as the author required. They never lacked clothes, meals, or comfortable beds. Their younger contemporary who died earlier, Edgar Allan Poe, struggled with poverty in that short life. The world did not recognize him as America's greatest writer until after his death. No other American has had such a strong influence on European literature. In 1909, the centenary of Poe's birth, from New York to Moscow, any writer with the power acknowledged that he or his country owed to Poe's genius.

Poe is above romance writers. He is the creator of novel, original short stories, and also a poet and critic. However, if there is no other reason except to say that the story of his life itself is romance, and Poe is a character in a real novel, and the main material of novels and dramas, then it is fair to regard him as a romance writer. The theme of that story is appealing to our feelings, whether or not it is specifically American, appealing to our feelings of praise for those who proceed in difficult circumstances. We in the business world, in the political world, like self-made people. Of course, no one is self-made, but if we interpret this term in the ordinary sense, we can call Poe a self-made writer. Needless to say, he was born with talent, but he struggled to maintain the purity of that talent, to develop it in disappointment and difficulty.

When Poe was twenty-four years old, he won a prize of one hundred gold dollars awarded by a newspaper in Baltimore, Maryland, for a short story called "MS. Found in a Bottle". Two points about this novel are noteworthy. This immediately showed Poe's ability to drive style and technique, and probably this was the only novel he got enough reward for. Why? Because Poe did not live his poor life by his most beautiful novels, and of course not by his poems, but by hard magazine work and rigid editorial affairs. He was a careful worker, and he could not do hasty work just for the sake of urgently waiting for money. The history of literature records many events about poverty and hardship and the sacrifice of material well-being for artistic ideals, but the glorious example of the literary profession, above Poe's example, does not exist. He was a man who proudly believed in his ability, and had the happy pride of knowing that his best works were stamped with immortality. It is inappropriate for those who lament his poverty, or complain that the world he lived in ignored genius, to complain. However, there is a small scene or fact that dramatizes his life. He had been a cadet at the United States Military Academy for several months. Sixteen years later, when his wife was dying, the only thing covering her bed was his military uniform.

Poe's novels describe mysterious realms and the influence of those realms on the human mind. His absorbing interest is in what is now becoming a thing called psychological habit. He created detective novels long before Sherlock Holmes and Arsène Lupin were born. In his view, detective novels are not at all a question of whether the criminal is arrested and punished. This is entirely a logical part of the mind, the question of how to act before the facts. He not only invented detective novels, the best ones being "The Purloined Letter" and "The Murders in the Rue Morgue," but also made the novel "The Mystery of Marie Roget" by taking an actual event that was not yet clear when he wrote it. The structure is almost no different from the real event. Later, it was determined that Poe was extremely proud of what he called his own reasoning power, believing and proving that whatever mystery, mechanical or intellectual, a person could conceive, others could always decompose it.

It is rare to see a poet and dreamer like Poe who has the ability to develop that ability for pure reason to such a high level among writers. This is not to say that there is something incompatible between reason and poetry, but quite the opposite. We know that Dante and Shakespeare and Goethe were capable in all thoughtful departments. However, it is rare for all kinds of abilities to be given to one person's mind. As time goes on, we are more and more sure to understand that Poe, whose brilliant heyday was interrupted before he reached the peak of his power, is a rare and supreme talent.

Poe's mysterious stories with ingenious reasoning, I am afraid, are clever tricks only. Although in three-quarters of the same century, no other writer was clever enough to surpass him. His most beautiful prose is not found in his creative stories, but in works that have a direct influence on emotions and feelings, like poetry or music. Works like "Ligeia" and "Shadow" are complete. If Poe was not the originator of that kind of prose poem, whatever original creation traces something that came before it is possible, then he is still the magician of that bewitching magic and there is no enemy, the poet Swinburne called Poe "always" thoroughly grinding out his own thoughts, from which he created or a solid, mature, and immortal thing. "A complete genius poet," Poe is complete in two senses. He brought his thoughts to the last form and completed them, and he had a great multi-faceted talent. His short stories are enough to give him fame, but even without that, he should also be remembered as a critic and poet.

Some of Poe's criticisms have lost their original interest because the books that aroused his criticism were of little value, and would have been forgotten without his criticism. However, even in the momentary criticisms in the newspapers, he often expressed a kind of thought with lasting value in literature. On the whole, his literary essays have more light and knowledge than any other American at that time. For general readers and specialized researchers, these are becoming the best narratives of American literature before 1850. He maintained the banner of exquisite works for himself and others in extremely unfavorable circumstances. For his immortal reputation, let him be remembered. He almost lifted his banner alone and proceeded, and it was extremely rare to have the courage and strength and a kind of proper modesty to follow his contemporaries. What makes Poe's residence in America and writing in America an eternally incomprehensible problem for European critics is no worse than the obscurity of his stories or the beauty of his poems. The superiority of his criticism is an example of the incomprehensible truth that great intelligence can be born in any environment. How or why such a thing happens, no one can explain. This is one of the living romantic mysteries that Poe himself cannot reason to a satisfactory conclusion.

Among the writers of the first half of the same century, there were people who were quite important at the time and are still memorable today, namely Mrs. Stowe, "Uncle Tom's Cabin" gave people an impression beyond what dreams or expectations she had when writing it. Lincoln tasted it with more than the precise courage of a historical figure and called her "a little lady who stirred up this great war." Tolstoy, who often seeks moral problems in novels, added it to the extremely limited list of books that he called true art. In my opinion, this seems to belong to second-rate art. Why? Because this is a special debate, propaganda, not raising the work to something that is so clear that it stimulates the urgent problem that sparked it. However, apart from or a kind of old-fashioned moral theory, this is not badly written. The story is vivid, and the pure passion triumphs over the vivid sentimentality.

After the Civil War, in the era of gradual maturity, there were three writers who occupied the first important position, and a few writers with less real value. The three were Mark Twain, Howells, and Henry James.

Theater News

The Guo Feng New Drama Society announces: The National Goods Department Store on Nanjing Road has now opened. In the Tong Le Amusement Park, there is an organization of our society. With such a lineup, it is certainly satisfactory. Li Ci Hang (also known as Jun Pan), who is in charge of the society's affairs, is also an advanced figure in spoken drama. Initially, he and Zhong Sheng Mu Duo, Ren Tian Zhi, and Lu Jing Ru, a key member of the Chun Liu Society, were all strong players who worked hard in new drama. In the first year of the Republic of China, they founded the Kai Ming New Drama Society, which achieved excellent results. Later, in Changsha, Hunan, and other places, he performed dramas with Gu Wu Wei, Chen Da Bei, and Zou Jian Hun.

He also had considerable prestige. However, in the past ten years, he has been almost isolated from the theater world. Although, when he is in the mood, he sometimes writes scripts. The play "Common Struggle," which he wrote when boycotting Japanese goods two years ago, was published in the Min Guo Daily. "Personality Problems," a one-act play published in the Red Rose magazine recently, is also his work. This time, because everyone is advocating domestic goods, he has also shown a little enthusiasm and accepted the invitation of the head of the amusement park to prepare to perform several dramas that promote domestic goods and promote national glory, fulfilling his duty of propaganda. At the same time, he wants to make another effort in theatrical arts, hoping to revive the declining new drama. However, he has been away from the stage for too long, and he is inevitably a little unfamiliar with the control of the drama. Therefore, he has specially invited Wu Ji Chen, who is experienced in this field, to serve as the director of choreography for the society. Wu has a solid foundation, rich thoughts, and creative specialties in drama. "Fragrant Grass in the Horizon" of the Min Xing Society and "The Maze on the Sea" of the Laughing Stage are his proud works. This time, he has assumed the position of director of choreography for the Guo Feng Society. With so many good actors on stage together, how handy it is!
